Background. Locally advanced bronchial tumors beyond stage IIB have long been considered a contraindication for surgery. However with advances in neoadjuvant therapy of NSCLC even locally advanced tumors in stage IIIA and IIB are potential candidates for surgery. Methods. We retrospectively reviewed all 72 patients who underwent curative resection of locally advanced NSCLC in stage T3 or T4 according to postoperative histology from 1=2002 to 12=2006. 19 patients received neoadjuvant chemotherapy, 7 patients neoadjuvant chemoradiotherapy. Adjuvant chemotherapy was performed in 10 patients, chemoradiotherapy in 9 patients and radiotherapy only also in 9 patients. Results. During the observation period 72 patients (14 females, 58 males; mean age 63 AE 10 years) with pT3=pT4 NSCLC underwent resection with curative intent. Postoperative stage was IIB in 23, IIIA in 17, IIIB in 27 and IV in 5 patients). In 61 patients R0 resection was achieved, in 9 patients histological R1 and in 2 patients macroscopic R2 residual tumor was left. Overall 30 day survival was 93.1%, 1 year survival 65.3% and 3 year survival 36.1%. Survival was significantly better if radical resection was achieved (p < 0.003). Those patients requiring ICU stay postoperative had a significantly worse outcome. Patients in stages IIIA and IIIB with neoadjuvant or adjuvant chemo-=radiotherapy had a comparable outcome to those patients in stage IIB. Conclusions. In a multimodality treatment including radical resection setting favourable outcome for patients with locally advanced NSCLC even in stages IIIA and IIIB can be achieved. Zur Behandlung der primären Hyperhidrose stehen konservative und operative Verfahren zur Verfügung. Während die thorakale Sympathektomie klinisch etabliert ist, wird die Bedeutung einer lumbalen Sympathektomie kontroversiell diskutiert. Methodik. Von September 2000 bis September 2007 wurden bei 204 Pat. 402 thorakoskopische Sympathektomien wegen palmarer (n ¼ 50), palmar=axillärer (n ¼ 107), axillärer (n ¼ 35) und kraniofazieller (n ¼ 12) Hyperhidrose und bei 68 Patienten 135 retroperitoneoskopische lumbale Sympathektomien wegen plantarer Hyperhidrose durchgeführt. Der Standardeingriff bei der thorakalen Sympathektomie bestand in einer T2 bis T4=T5 Resektion und bei der lumbalen in einer L3 und=oder L4 Resektion. Ergebnisse. Die Letalität betrug 0%, die Morbidität nach thorakaler Sympathektomie 2,5% (10=402) und nach lumbaler 1,5% (2=135). Bei keinem Patienten kam es zu einer Sexualfunktionsstörung. Postoperativ war die Hyperhidrose in allen Zielregionen eliminiert. 196 Pat. (215 Hände, 214 Axillen,105 Füsse) wurden nachuntersucht (median 21 Mo). Die palmare Hyperhidrose war in allen Fällen (100%) die axilläre Hyperhidrose in 211 (98,6%) und die plantare Hyperhidrose in 103 (98%) beseitigt. Nach lumbaler Sympathektomie kam es bei 4% der Pat. zu einem starken kompensatorischen Schwitzen, 93% waren mit dem Ergebnis sehr zufrieden und 96% würden den Eingriff wieder durchführen lassen. Nach thorakaler Sympathektomie lagen die Werte in der Gruppe mit palmar=axillärer Hyperhidrose bei 16%, 92% und 94% und bei Pat. mit rein axillärer Hyperhidrose bei 53%, 47% und 66%. Schlussfolgerungen. Die palmare und plantare Hyperhidrose ist sicher und effektiv mittels thorakaler und lumbaler Sympathektomie zu behandeln. Bei Pat. mit axillärer Hyperhidrose sollte wegen der hohen Rate an starkem kompensatorischen Schwitzen anderen Therapieverfahren der Vorzug gegeben werden. Outcome of endothoracic sympathetic block at T4 for axillary hyperhidrosis Background. Endoscopic thoracic sympathetic block (ETSB) provides excellent long-term outcome for palmar hyperhidrosis (HH), but results for axillary HH have been worse (failure= recurrence rate 65%). The aim of the study was to investigate the effect of ETSB4 on axillary HH. Methods. Between 2002 and 2006 82 patients (58 females; mean age 30.2 years AE9.3) with severe axillary and palmaraxillary HH were treated by clip application above and below the T4 ganglion. Outcome and quality-of-life analysis (Qol) were assessed by VAS scores ranging from 1-10 and 1-5, respectively. Mean follow up was 19.2 AE 11.0 months. Results. Nine patients (11.0%) had isolated axillary and 73 (89.0%) palmar-axillary HH. Sixty-one patients (74.4%) had dry and 17 (20.7%) improved armpits, whereas 4 (4.9%) were humid at follow-up (3 primary failures, 1 recurrence). Compensatory sweating (CS) was found in 29 patients (35.4%), but none considered it as unbearable. Qol scores improved from 8.43 AE 2.20 to 1.36 AE 0.51 (Keller, p < 0.001) and from 4.53 AE 0.74 to 1.50 AE 0.82 (Milanez de Campos, p < 0.013). 71 patients (86.6%) were completely and 8 (9.8%) partly satisfied. 96.3% would recommend the operation. Two patients (2.4%) with CS and one (1.2%) suffering from recurrence were not satisfied. Conclusions. ETSB4 results in acceptable midterm results for patients with axillary HH. The restrictive attitude for sympathetic surgery in case of axillary HH should be reconsidered as alternative therapeutic options have also considerable disadvantages (short-term effect of botulinum toxin, 100% recurrence after sweat gland suction within 2 years). Effect of endothoracic sympathectomy on vascular disorders P. T. Panhofer 1 , J. Zacherl 1 , T. Hölzenbein 2 , M. Prager 3 , R. Jakesz 1 , G. Bischof 4 , C. Neumayer 1 Background. Endoscopic thoracic sympathectomy (ETS) has been used for treatment of vascular disorders of the upper limb. However, reports on limited number of patients gave controversial results. The aim of our study was to analyze the effect of ETS on patients with vaso-spastic and -occlusive diseases. Methods. Between 1965 and 2004 59 patients underwent 89 ETS procedures. 32 patients had primary, 17 secondary Raynaud's disease and 9 had vaso-occlusive diseases (including 5 patients with Buerger's disease) and one patients suffered from thromboembolic ischemia. Median follow-up was 12 years, available from 15 patients, 15 patients had died from cardiovascular events and further 30 patients have been lost. Results. 16.8% had minor (primarily subcutaneous emphysema and residual pneumothorax) and 2.2% major morbidities (one patient with temporary ptosis, one with stenocardia). 75% of patients reported subjective improvement lasting for 6 to 8 months. Most of the patients had already finger tip necroses at time of operation. Nevertheless, ulcer healing rate was 64%. Moreover, intractable pain was diminished in all of the patients (9.6 AE 0.4 before ETS versus 2.4 AE 0.5 after ETS, p < 0.05) as assessed by a visual analogue scale from 0 (no pain) to 10 (maximal pain). Conclusions. Endoscopic thoracic sympathectomy can be recommended for patients with limb threatening end-stage upper limb vascular disorders. Although the vasodilatory effect is not long-lasting, a high rate of healed necrotic digits and pain relief in all of the patients are convincing arguments for this surgical procedure. Treatment of cervical lymph node tuberculosis by radical neck dissection and subsequent V.A.C. + therapy Grundlagen. Der Patchinfekt ist eine seltene jedoch sehr gefürchtete Komplikation nach Carotis-Thrombendarteriektomie (TEA). Er kann zu chronischen Wundinfekten, Pseudoaneurysmen mit Gefahr der Embolisation und zur sekundären Ruptur führen. Fallbericht. Wir berichten von einem 64-jährigen Patienten, der vor 5 Jahren wegen einer hochgradigen Arteria Carotis Interna (ACI)-Stenose eine TEA und Patchplastik der rechten ACI erhalten hat. Der postoperative Verlauf gestaltete sich unauffällig. Vor eineinhalb Jahren wurde der Patient wegen einer plötzlichen Schwellung im Bereich der alten Narbe vorstellig. In der durchgeführten MRT zeigte sich eine phlegmonöse Entzündung im Bereich des M. Sternocleidomastoideus ohne Hinweis auf Gefäßbeteiligung. Unter einer antibiotischen Therapie kam es primär zu einer weitestgehenden Abheilung. Aufgrund von persistierender Lymphknotenschwellung im Narbenbereich erfolgte eine LK-PE ohne fassbares histologisches Ergebnis. Nach zwei oberflächlichen Wundrevisionen ohne Hinweis auf Beteiligung tieferer Strukturen erfolgte schlussendlich aufgrund persistierender Beschwerden eine neuerliche Revision mit genauer Gefäßdarstellung. Es zeigte sich der Patch gewellt mit teilweise gelöster Naht und nicht mit dem Umgebungsgewebe verwachsen. Der infizierte Patch wurde durch einen autologen Saphena-Patch ersetzt und die Wunde genauestens debridiert. Eine unmittelbar postoperativ aufgetretene Blutung im kranialen Anteil der Carotis interna, die aufgrund der Brüchigkeit des Gefäßes nur unter einer höhergradigen Stenosierung des Gefäßes versorgt werden konnte, wurde unmittelbar postoperativ interventionell gedehnt und mittels eines gecoverten Stents gesichert. Der weitere postoperative Verlauf gestaltete sich komplikationslos. Schlussfolgerungen. Bei chronische rezidivierenden Weichteilinfekten im Narbenbereich nach Carotis-TEA sollte auch bei negativer Bildgebung an einen Patchinfekt gedacht werden. Die einzige kurative Therapie ist der Ersatz des infizierten Kunststoffpatches durch einen autologen Venenpatch. Minimal invasive Chirurgie in der aortoiliacalen Gefäßchirurgieeigene Erfahrungen R. Zwrtek, H. Hackstock, N. Spitzer, G. Salem Abteilung für Allgemein-, Gefäß-und Thoraxchirurgie, Landesklinikum St. Pölten, St. Pölten, Österreich Neben den klassischen offenen Operationsmethoden und den interventionell-endovaskulären Behandlungen hat sich auch die minimal invasive Chirurgie in der Gefäßchirurgie entwickelt. Es wird die schrittweise Einführung der Methode in unserem Haus beschrieben. Das erste Problem stellt die Exposition der Aorta und Iliacalgefäße dar. Durch spezielle Lagerung und Seitendrehung des Patienten und dem transperitonealem retrocolischen Zugang konnte die Aortenexposition wesentlich vereinfacht werden. Neue technisch apparative Entwicklungen der Gasinsufflation, laparoskopieadaptierte Dissektionsgeräte und Spezialinstrumentarium erleichtern die Präparation zusätzlich. Das zweite große Problem -die Anastomosierung -haben wir versucht, in 2 Schritten zu lösen. Zunächst wurde die Anastomose über eine Minilaparotomie (max. 8 cm Hautschnitt) angelegt. Schon dies führte zu einer deutlichen Reduktion perioperativer Komplikationen. Die komplett laparoskopisch durchgeführte Anastomose ist technisch anspruchsvoll und benötigt intensives Training. Lange Klemmzeiten, mit ihren bekannten negativen Auswirkungen, stellen das große Hindernis dar. Wir haben uns daher zunächst entschieden, komplett laparoskopische Anastomosen nur bei Patienten mit okklusiven aorto-iliacalen Prozessen durchzuführen. Die Operationszeiten sind je nach Lernkurve früher oder später im akzeptablen Bereich, jedoch selbstverständlich länger als bei offenen Operationsmethoden. Die Vorteile der MIC sind vor allem geringere postoperative Schmerzen, Vermeiden postoperativer Paralyse und das Auftreten weniger Narbenhernien. Genaue Zahlen können beim Kongress präsentiert werden. Die MIC im Bereich der Aneurysmachirurgie betrachten wir derzeit noch kritisch. Die Anzahl der AAA, die für eine laparoskopische Operation in Frage kommen sind in unserem Krankengut gering. Die richtige Patientenselektion für MIC, offener aorto-iliacaler Rekonstruktionen oder extraanatomischer Bypassverfahren ist eine ebenso große Herausforderung wie die technische Machbarkeit der Laparoskopie. Grundlagen. Vaskuläre Komplikationen der ERCP sind in der Literatur bislang nicht beschrieben worden. Fallbericht. Wir berichten über eine septische Arrosionsblutung der A. iliaca com. dext. bei einem 51 jährigen Mann nach Dislokation eines Pancreasstent in die Pars horizontalis inferior des Duodenums. Der Stent wurde daraufhin endoskopisch entfernt. In weiterer Folge entwicklelte der Patient eine massive gastrointestinale Blutung, welche eine notfallsmäßigen Laparotomie erforderte. Das untere Duodenalknie wurde primär übernäht und die Blutung aus der A. iliaca communis behelfsmäßig gestillt. Anschließend entwickelte sich ein septisches Pseudoaneurysma der A. iliaca mit Embolisation in die Unterschenkelarterien, welches durch eine transfemorale Stentgraftimplantation behandelt wurde. Postoperativ erhielt der Patient eine antibiotische Langzeittherapie. Schlussfolgerungen. Primäre intestino-arterielle Fisteln zu größerkalibrigen Arterien ohne vorangegange gefäßchirurgische Intervention sind in der Literatur nur als Einzelkasuistiken zu finden. Cohnert 1 Grundlagen. Die Endarterektomie der A. carotis interna ist bei hämodynamisch signifikanten Stenosen eine Operation mit Evidenzlevel A. Exklusionskriterien: medikamentös therapierter Diabetes mellitus, schwere, vorbestehende Augenerkrankungen. Ergebnisse (Zwischenauswertung nach 8 Fällen). Pt. 1: präoperativ o.B., postoperativ temporale Gesichtsfeldeinschränkung am kontralateralen Auge, Pt. 2: präoparativ o.B., postoperativ temporale Gesichtsfeldeinschränkung auf der operierten Seite, Pt. 3: präoperativ konzentrische Gesichtsfeldeinschränkung, postoperativ o.B., Pt. 4: präoperativ temporale Gesichtsfeldeinschränkung, postoperativ idem, Pt. 5: präoperativ konzentrische Gesichtsfeldeinschränkung, postoperativ o.B., Pt. 6-8: prä-und postoperativ o.B. Schlussfolgerungen. Unsere nächste Untersuchung wird sich mit der Frage beschäftigen, ob es Perfusionskonstellationen gibt, welche prädiktiv für Typ A bzw. für Typ B Veränderungen sind. Ergebnisse. Es gab keine intra-oder postoperativen Komplikationen. Die OP-Zeit war in der Lasergruppe kü rzer. Bei 117 gelang ein komplettes Follow up. 22 Patienten wurden mittels Laser, 95 konventionell behandelt. Die Gruppen wurden zu Baseline auf Unterschied getestet, sie unterscheiden sich nicht voneinander. Präoperativ unterscheiden sich die Gruppen auch hinsichtlich SF-36 und Aberdeen score nicht voneinander. 3 Monate postoperativ zeigten die Gruppen in sich statistisch signifikante Verbesserungen: Laser: bei physical function; Stripping: bei physical function, role physical and bodily pain. Keine der beiden Gruppen zeigt eine statistisch signifikante größere Veränderung als die andere -im Vergleich unterscheiden sich die beiden Gruppen 3 Monate postop. nicht. Gleiches zeigte der Aberdeen score. Schlussfolgerungen. Bei entsprechender Indikationsstellung kommt es nach Sanierung der Stammvene mittels Stripping oder endoluminaler Obliteration zur Verbesserung der Lebensqualität. 3 Monate postoperativ unterscheiden sich die beiden Verfahren hinsichtlich Qol nicht voneinander. Einleitung. Die Carotisendarterektomie kurz nach einem Schlaganfall wurde noch vor wenigen Jahren als Kontraindikation für eine sofortige operative Sanierung bei gleichzeitigem Vorliegen einer ipsilateralen hochgradigen Arteria carotis interna Stenose wegen hohem Einblutungsrisiko im ischämischen Schlaganfallareal angesehen. Insultpatienten wurden vielerorts sechs Wochen ,,abgekühlt'', bevor sie einer operativen Sanierung zugeführt wurden. Derzeit werden an vielen gefäßchirurgischen Zentren Patienten mit rezentem ischämischen Schlaganfall, in Absprache mit den Fachärzten für Neurologie, einer sofortigen Carotisendarterektomie unterzogen. Wir berichten über die Ergebnisse dieses Patientengutes am Herz-und Gefäßzentrum Hietzing der Stadt Wien. Material und methoden. Ab 2006 werden unsere CAVK-Patienten im VASCULAR Qualitätssicherungsprogramm (vorgestellt anlässlich des International Vascular Workshop 2007=Going) erfasst. Bis dato wurden 302 Carotisendarterektomien dokumentiert. 4 Patienten wurden im klinischen Stadium IIIB und 24 Patienten kurzfristig nach manifestem Insult im CAVK Stadium IV operiert. Der Zeitraum zwischen den im CCT oder Schädel-MRT diagnostizierten cerebralen ischämischen Insulten und der operativen Sanierung betrug zwischen neun Stunden und, je nach zuweisendem Zentrum, bis zu drei Wochen. Die Thrombendarterektomie mit Venen-oder Kunststoffpatch erfolgte ausnahmslos in Allgemeinnarkose mit intraoperativer Shunteinlage. Zwanzig der Patienten wurden zur besseren Ü berwachung an unsere Intensivstation transferiert. Acht Patienten kamen postoperativ an die Stroke-Unit unserer neurologischen Abteilung. 70% aller Patienten wurden unter Dauertherapie mit Thrombozytenfunktionshemmern operiert. Ergebnisse. Die perioperative Mortalität im gesamten Krankengut betrug 0,33%. Ein Patient (CAVK Stadium IIB) verstarb im Rahmen des stationären Aufenthaltes an den Folgen eines post-operativ aufgetretenen Myocardinfarktes. Die perioperativen neurologischen Komplikationen betrugen insgesamt 2,2%. Es trat ein postoperativer ipsilateraler Insult (CAVK Stadium IIA), ein kontralateraler Insult (CAVK Stadium IA) und fünf prolongierte ischämische neurologische Defizite (dreimal CAVK Stadium IIB, zweimal CAVK Stadium IB, mit kompletter Restitution bei Entlassung), auf. Drei Patienten mussten wegen Nachblutung chirurgisch revidiert werden. Bei einem Patienten (CAVK Stadium IA) kam es postoperativ zu einem asymptomatischen Verschluß der operierten Arteria carotis interna. Die Eingriffe der Patienten im CAVK Stadium IIIA þ B und IV verliefen komplikationslos. Zusammenfassung. Die umgehende operative Sanierung von Patienten im akuten Schlaganfall und kurzfristig nach manifestem Insult vergesellschaftet mit einer ipsilateralen hochgradigen Stenose der Arteria carotis interna, hat sich an unserer Abteilung bewährt. Es gab im Vergleich mit Patienten im CAVK Stadium I und II keine erhöhte perioperative Morbidität und= oder Mortalität. In Zusammenarbeit mit den neurologischen Zentren unseres Hauses konnte bei den im CAVK Stadium IV operierten Patienten eine signifikant schnellere Rückbildung der neurologischen Symptomatik beobachtet werden. Methodik. Von 1=01 bis 9=07 wurden an unserer Abteilung n ¼ 139 Pankreasresektionen durchgeführt (n ¼ 73 Frauen, n ¼ 66 Männer, mittleres Alter 64 Jahre). Die Daten wurden prospektiv erfasst, zur Identifizierung von Risikofaktoren für Mortalität und Morbidität wurde eine Regressionsanalyse durchgeführt. Ergebnisse. Indikation zur Operation waren n ¼ 85 maligne und n ¼ 54 benigne Erkrankungen (n ¼ 60 Pankreaskarzinom, n ¼ 4 neuroendokriner Tumor, n ¼ 21 sonstiges Malignom, n ¼ 29 chronische Pankreatitis, n ¼ 25 benigner Tumor). Die Resektion wurde in 99 Fällen als pyloruserhaltende Duodenopankreatektomie, in 4 Fällen als klassische Whipple-Operation durchgefü hrt, weiters 2 totale Pankreatektomien, eine zentrale Resektion, eine Enukleation und 32 Pankreaslinksresektionen. Die Mortalität betrug n ¼ 3=139 (2,16%), die Morbidität n ¼ 35=139 (25,18%), die Relaparotomierate n ¼ 14= 139 (10,07%). Die häufigsten postoperativen Komplikationen waren Pankreasfisteln und Spätblutungen. Bei Grundlagen. Die Evaluation von POK erlaubt einem chirurgischem Ausbildungskrankenhaus die Qualität der Pflege und der Ausbildung zu kontrollieren. Diese aus der prospektiven Sammlung erhaltenen Daten der POK sind nach einer einfachen Methode klassifiziert. Klassifizierungen. Komplikationen Typ I: keine Behandlung. IIm: einfache internistische Behandlung. IIs: chirurgische Behandlung am Patientenbett. IIIm: internistisches Problem mit Verlegung auf Intensivstation. IIIs: chirurgisches Problem mit Wiedereingriff im OP. IV: Verlust eines Organs oder seiner Funktion. Typ V: Patiententod. Zur besseren POKerfassung, wurden diese in direkte, indirekte (mit=ohne Zusammenhang mit dem Eingriff) oder unter ,,Fortschritt der Grundkrankheit'' klassifiziert. Methodik. Seit Juli 1995 wurden 17.100 Patienten operiert und in unsere prospektive Studie eingeschlossen. Die POK sind wöchentlich notiert, analysiert und untergliedert worden nach Schweregrad, ihrer Ä tiologie und ihrer Behandlung. Ergebnisse. Von 17.100 Patienten haben insgesamt 12,9% (2049 Patienten) eine oder mehrere POK gehabt mit 3674 Komplikationen. Mehr als die Hälfte waren vom Typ I (8,9%), IIm (32%), IIIm (7,9%). Bei 36,6% waren POK vom Typ IIs (16,9%) und IIIs (19,7%). Von 171 Patienten mit Typ IV hatten 43% keinen direkten Zusammenhang mit dem Eingriff. Bei Typ V (5,8%) waren die Gründe meist kardio-pulmonalen Ursprungs. Schlussfolgerungen. Die prospektive Analyse von POK zeigt, dass annähernd die Hälfte davon internistisch sind und dass für die Typ IIs, IIIs und IV der Faktor der Krankheitsprogression der zugrundeliegenden Krankheit nicht unwesentlich ist. Diese Studie hat uns erlaubt, die Qualität der Pflege zu kontrollieren und bestimmte chirurgische Behandlungen zu verbessern. Wichtigste Risikofaktoren sind Herz-Kreislauf-Krankheiten, Ü bergewicht und Diabetes. The importance of non-technical skills for surgical quality Computer-based medical simulation provides a realistic and economical set of tools to improve and maintain the skills of health care providers adding a valuable dimension to medical training. Medical simulators allow individuals to review and practice procedures as often as required to reach proficiency without harming the patient. Optimistic forecasts predicted rapid adoption of medical simulation, even using them as platforms for certification: Many medical schools around the world are currently providing ''hands on'' health care education to medical students and postgraduate training. Practicing on cadavers, laboratory animals, or real patients has been the only way to teach them about anatomy and how to practice medicine. Moreover, there is growing recognition that medical error is most often a consequence of system error where normal checks and balances do not succeed in mitigating error or harm. Simulation-based Medical Education (SBME) includes several tools and approaches, for example: The question ''Why we should use medical simulation?'' is best answered on the homepage of Advanced Initiative in Medical Simulation: One of the most exciting innovations in health care is in the field of medical simulation. Let us change our system and use medical simulation in training and continuous medical education. Employing medical simulation techniques can help move medicine from the old ''see one, do one, teach one'' method to a ''see one, practice many, do one'' model for success. Grundlagen. Scaphoidfrakturen beim Kind unter 10 Jahren sind eine Rarität und finden eine Häufung um das 15. Lebensjahr. In der Anamnese findet sich typischerweise ein Sturz auf die hyperextendierte Hand. Bei dislozierten Brüchen besteht die Indikation zur operativen Versorgung. Eine Durchblutungsstörung vor allem bei proximalen Polbrüchen stellt in dieser Altersgruppe eine Ausnahme dar. Primär übersehene Frakturen werden häufig verspätet im Stadium der Pseudarthrose aufgrund persistierneder Beschwerden diagnostiziert. Methodik. Alle Patienten mit der Diagnose einer Kahnbeinfraktur oder Kahnbeinpseudarthrose aus dem Zeitraum 2004 bis 2007 wurden retrospektiv analysiert. Die Bewertung des funktionellen Ergebnisses erfolgte nach dem DASH-Score (Disabilities of the Arm, Shoulder and Hand). Zur Beurteilung möglicher nativradilogischer Veränderungen wurde die Bildgebung der letztmaligen ambulanten Vorstellung herangezogen. Ergebnisse. In drei Jahren wurden 69 Kahnbeinverletzungen behandelt. Es fanden sich 57 männliche und 12 weibliche Patienten. Das Durchschnittsalter betrug 14,4 Jahre. Eine operative Intervention war bei sieben Patienten indiziert. Zwei Frakturen zeigten nach einer frischen Verletzung eine Dislokation beziehungsweise Diastase von mehr als 2 mm. In order to reduce the amount of motion it is recommended to use the shortest possible loop length. Background. Modalities available for the diagnosis of hepatic injuries include focused abdominal sonography for trauma (FAST) , computed tomography (CT) and liver function tests (LFT's) . In this study the diagnostic value of CT and LFT's was evaluated. Methods. Medical records of all patients with liver injuries managed in our institution in the past 7 years were reviewed for trauma mechanism, grade of liver trauma, diagnostic and therapeutic management. Preoperative diagnosis was compared to intraoperative findings. Results. From 2000 to 2007 a total of 101 patients with liver trauma were managed in our trauma unit. 19 (18.8%) patients were hemodynamically unstable and therefore underwent immediate laparotomy without further imaging. 82 patients were admitted in hemodynamically stable condition and underwent contrast enhanced spiral CT, 30 patients required surgery the same day allowing direct comparison of CT diagnosis and intraoperative findings. Overall, CT had a sensitivity of 81.5% (22 of 27 patients), a specificity of 93.1% (27 of 29 patients) and a positive predictive value of 91% (21 of 23 patients). Mean ALT was 64.2U=l for grade I, 222.2 for grade II, 364.7 for grade III, 559.3 for grade IV and 362.3 for grade V injuries, respectively. Eleven patients with liver trauma had normal LFT's. Conclusions. Computed tomography is a very useful tool in the detection and evaluation of liver trauma, however its sensitivity is often overestimated. LFT's are sensitive and specific markers for blunt hepatic injuries and its role in diagnosis and follow up needs to be redefined. Successful management of osteosynthesis infection caused by Enterococcus faecium after severe leg trauma W. Tabarelli 1 , H. Bonatti 2 , K. Benedetto 1 , O. Naumann 1 1 Academic Hospital, Feldkirch, Austria; 2 University of Virginia Health Systems, Charlottesville, USA Background. Infection of alloplastic material is usually caused by staphylococci. Enterococci rarely have been implicated in infections after osetosythesis. Enterococcus faecium is resistant to most antibiotics with glycopeptides being considered treatment of choice. Case report. A 41-year-old male experienced severe trauma during a working accident with multiple open fractures of the right femur, tibia, food and toes. Initial treatment included stabilizing the fractures using external fixation and debridement of wounds with application of a vacuum assisted device. On the third day post trauma the fracture was stabilized by osteosynthesis of the median condyle. Repeatedly, soft tissue necroses were debrided and the VAC-system changed and after four weeks the skin was covered with a MESH graft. During the seventh week the patient experienced a fracture of the LISS and a new system had to be implanted. Enterococcus faecium was isolated and treatment was started with Vancomycin. The patient underwent another two surgical intervention with debridement of necrosis and implantation of autologous spongiosa and osigraft. External fixation was removed and moderate mechanical stress was tolerated. Antibiotic therapy was switched to oral linezolid for another six weeks. Nine weeks later, CT scan showed a regenerated femur and ankle joint. Six months following the complicated trauma, the patient was able to walk again. Conclusions. Multimodal approach with stepwise reconstruction of the severely traumatized tissue allowed recovery from this injury with a good functional result. Linezolid proved useful in the oral therapy of this severe enterococcal infection. Background. MET tyrosine kinase inhibition is an emerging strategy for tumors with genomic amplification of MET. Several MET inhibitors have entered clinical trials, however, potential resistance mechanisms remain to be elucidated. Methods. Recent evidence suggests that alternative growth factor receptor pathway activation mediates resistance to receptor tyrosine kinase inhibition. We hypothesized that stimulation of the epidermal growth factor receptor (EGFR) or HER-3 pathways are mechanisms by which MET-amplified tumor cells can be rescued from the effects of MET inhibition. Results. Treatment of MET-amplified gastric cancer cells with the MET tyrosine kinase inhibitor PHA-665752 abrogated Ras= Raf=MEK=mitogen-activated protein kinase (MAPK) and phosphoinositide-3-kinase (PI3K)=AKT signaling, leading to cyclin D1 loss and G1-arrest. PHA-665752 also abrogated baseline phosphorylation of EGFR and HER-3, which are transactivated by MET in these cells. Restimulation of EGFR with EGF, or HER-3 with heregulin-1 (HRG) rescued the cells from the growth-inhibitory effects of PHA-665752 by reactivating either the MAPK pathway (EGF) or both the MAPK and PI3K pathways (HRG). While inhibition of MAPK signaling alone counteracted the EGF rescue effect in PHA-665752-treated cells, only combined inhibition of MAPK and PI3K signaling could counteract the HRG rescue effect. The effects of both ligands in PHA-665752-treated cells could be abrogated by the EGFR tyrosine kinase inhibitor gefitinib. Conclusions. Stimulation of EGFR with EGF, or HER-3 with HRG mediates resistance to MET inhibition. Combined inhibition of MET and EGFR=HER-3 signaling offers the possibility to prevent such resistance, making it a promising approach for MET-amplified tumors coexpressing EGFR and=or HER-3. Lipocalin-2 expression is associated with metastatic potential of colon cancer Background. Lipocalin-2 (Lcn-2, NGAL) was recently shown to be highly expressed in various human cancers and increased protein levels were significantly associated with worse overall survival of patients with breast, gastric or oesophageal cancer. The main focus of this work was to analyze the possible implication of Lcn-2 upregulation in colon cancer development and metastasis. Methods. Expression of Lcn-2 was analyzed in various colorectal carcinoma cell lines, paired colorectal carcinoma tissues and normal mucosas by Western blot. Lcn-2 immunostaining was performed in 98 colorectal carcinoma resection specimens (Intensity score 0-3) and correlated with clinical parameters. Colorectal carcinoma cell lines were treated with various concentrations of recombinant Lcn-2 protein and monitored for growth and survival by CKK Assay. Results. Western blot analysis of colorectal carcinoma cell lines and tissues clearly demonstrated Lcn-2 overexpression in carcinomas compared with normal mucosas in all colorectal carcinoma tissue pairs analysed. Immunostaining revealed Lcn-2 overexpression in 88 (89.8%) of colorectal carcinoma tissues. Intense immunoreactivity was significantly correlated with tumor metastasis (p < 0.046). Addition of various concentrations of recombinant human Lcn-2 protein to colorectal carcinoma cell lines did not have any influence on cell growth and survival in vitro. Conclusions. Our data provide evidence that Lcn-2 expression is upregulated with tumor progression. The increase of Lcn-2 expression in patients with colon cancer metastasis shed light on a possible function of Lcn-2 in tumorgenesis and as an indicator for metastatic potential. Thus, targeting Lcn-2 might be a new therapeutic strategy in colorectal carcinoma. Blocking of RET oncogen-triggered pathways by sorafenib stops progression of disease in metastatic medullary cancer patients Background. RET receptor tyrosin kinase activity plays a major role in medullary thyroid cancer (MTC) tumor growth. Sorafenib is an oral agent that selectively targets RET tyrosine kinases. Methods. Five patients with metastatic MTC with excessive elevation of calcitonin (CTN) serum levels entered this pilot study. Hypercalcitonemia-related symptoms were present in all patients (3 severe diarrhea, 2 moderate) and metastasisrelated symptoms were present in 4 (2 severe pain, 2 moderate). All patients had had prior adequate surgery, 4 had prior octreotide therapy, 3 chemotherapy. They received 800 mg or 400 mg (weight < 50 kg) Sorafenib as a starting dose. Dosage was reduced gradually in 200 mg scale when patients revealed therapy induced side effects to avoid worsening of quality of life. The scheduled duration of therapy was 6 months. Results. After 3 months CTN decreased to levels > 50% of baseline in all patients, to levels > 90% in 2. According to that all patients were free of CTN related symptoms after 4 weeks. CEA levels reacted in a similar way. Controls of metastatic lesions were classified as CR -1, PR -1, NC -3 pats. 2 patients with severe metastasis-related pain were off analgesics after 3 months of treatment. Due to side effects, Sorafenib dosage was reduced to 50% of the initial dose in all. All patients are on therapy 18-12 months after initiation, no progression of disease was detected. Conclusions. Sorafenib has to be considered as an effective treatment of symptomatic, metastatic MTC. Grundlagen. Reactivity of integrin-linked kinase and the recurrence of NSCLC after bronchoplastic resection Background. The pattern of recurrence after bronchoplastic procedures cannot be explained by histological stage alone; therefore, the search for genetic characteristics of the primary tumor is justified. Integrin-linked kinase (ILK) is a protein kinase that links the cell-adhesion receptors, integrins and growth factors to a range of signaling pathways. ILK activity is increased in a variety of human cancers. The role of ILK in local and distant relapse after bronchoplastic procedures for NSCLC is unknown. Methods. Tumor samples of 47 patients with NSCLC histology treated by bronchoplastic resection techniques were stained with a polyclonal antibody against ILK-1. The intensity of staining was evaluated by two independent observers blinded against the clinical follow-up. ILK expression, mean survival and patterns of recurrence were statistically correlated. Results. The mean overall survival of ILK-negative patients was 59 months, as compared to 37 months in ILK-positive patients (p ¼ 0.031). Freedom from distant recurrence was observed in 71% of patients with ILK-negative and in only 29% of patients with ILK-positive NSCLCs (p ¼ 0.027). On the other hand, the incidence of local recurrence was not correlated with ILK-status. Conclusions. In this study we show for the first time that the expression of ILK in NSCLC tumors is positively correlated with a higher risk of distant recurrence as compared to ILK-negative cases. ILK status does not impact on local recurrence. Hence, ILK-positive NSCLC may be treated by means of bronchoplastic procedures, but could particularly benefit from concomitant chemotherapy. Due to increasing life expectancy in industrialized countries, the number of octogenarian patients undergoing an open heart procedure is increasing. In these patients with high comorbidity less invasive procedures could probably improve the postoperative outcome. The aim of this study was to determine the effects of minimal access aortic valve replacement (AVR) in octogenarians on postoperative morbidity and mortality. Methods. Partial upper sternotomy has become the standard approach to isolated aortic valve surgery at our institution. Allmost 20% of the 353 patients who underwent AVR through a partial upper sternotomy between 1998 and 2006 were octogenarians. We reviewed retrospectively data on these patients. Results. The patients had a mean logistic Euroscore of 9.1 (0.9-29.2) and a mean left ventricular ejection fraction of 54.7% (20-70%). Mean cross clamp time and mean bypass time were 63.3 min (33-149 min) and 108.5 min (52-290 min), respectively. In 3 patients (4.3%) a conversion into full median sternotomy was necessary due to bleeding (n ¼ 2) and low cardiac output (n ¼ 1). Mean ICU and total hospital stay were 2.8 and 11.7 days, respectively. Postoperative bleeding complications were not observed. Deep sternum infection occured in 2 patients (2.8%). None of the patients had to be reoperated for prosthetic valve dysfunction or endocarditis. The hospital mortality rate was 5.7%. Conclusions. AVR through a partial upper sternotomy in octagenarians is a safe and effective technique with less invasivity resulting in satisfying postoperative morbidity and mortality. Minimally invasive aortic valve replacement through right mini-thoracotomythe Innsbruck experience Background. In the last decade minimally invasive surgical techniques were introduced into cardiac surgery. Aortic valve replacement through a right mini-thoracotomy has been established in November 2006 in our department. Methods. Until January 2008 we have included 31 patients, who were eligible for minimally invasive aortic valve replacement. Exclusion criteria were additional cardiac surgical interventions, severe pulmonary hypertension, important COPD. All patients received a preoperative 3-dimensional CT scan for evaluation of anatomy and ascending aortic disease. Results. Median age was 71 years, ranging from 54 to 89 years, median BMI 27 (22 to 34). The underlying diagnosis was aortic stenosis in 28 (90%) and regurgitation in 3 patients (10%). Median peak-to-peak gradient in aortic stenosis was 81 mmHg, ranging from 51 to 110 mmHg. Median EF was 52% (28 to 81%). 4 Patients (13%) received a mechanical and 27 (87%) a biological prosthesis. Median prosthesis size was 23 mm (19 to 25 mm). Patients received a mean of 0.25 packs of red cells perioperatively. Median cross clamping time was 96 min, (54 to 139), and median cardiopulmonary bypass time was 153 min, (85 to 224). One patient (3%) died due to perioperative myocardial infarction. Conclusions. Several recognized advantages (small skin incision, minimal blood loss, fast postoperative recovery) compared to disadvantages (longer operating time, challenging surgical technique) favor minimally invasive aortic valve replacement through a right minithoracotomy in carefully selected patients compared to median sternotomy. Pediatric heart transplantationthe Innsbruck experience J. Kilo, D. Höfer, R. Geiger, U. Schweigmann, G. Laufer, H. Antretter Background. Cardiac transplantation (HTX) is an accepted treatment of terminal heart failure in adults. In childhood, however, a number of congenital as well as aqcuired diseases may also lead to terminal heart failure. The aim of our study was to investigate the results of pediatric HTX at our department. Methods. We investigated on all pediatric HTX performed in Innsbruck between 1996 and 2007 . Demographic aspects, cardiac disease, waiting time, bridging devices as well as outcome were evaluated. Results. From 1996 through 2007, 16 HTX were performed in 15 children at our departement. Nine children were males, 6 females. Mean age was 10.3 years with a range from 0.8 to 18 years. Underlying cardiac disease was a dilative cardiomyopathy in 9 children, restrictive cardiomyopathy in 2. One transplantation was performed for Ebsteins' anomaly, one for virus myocarditis and one for muscular dystrophia. One girl, who was first transplanted in 1996, underwent retransplantation for TX-vasculopathy in 2007. Furthermore, one boy underwent retransplantation, who was first transplanted elsewhere. Mean waiting time was 177 days with a range from 4 to 652 days. One girl died on first postoperative day due to peracute rejection. No further deaths were encountered in postoperative course so far. Mechanical bridging systems were used in nine children. These include one ECMO, two LVADs and six BVADs. Conclusions. HTX is a good therapeutical option for children suffering from terminal heart failure, leading to good long-term results with acceptable perioperative risk. Active endocarditis of heart valves is still a serious problem in cardiac surgery. Furthermore the choice of valvular substitute and=or repair techniques respectively can be challenging. Methods. We report the case of a patient with pacemakerlead associated tricuspid valve endocarditis who had several re-interventions due to lead misfunctions in previous years. Concomitant coronary bypass grafting was indicated. The tricuspid valve was repaired after all the leads and the infectious thrombus-formation have been removed. The septal leaflet was patched with bovine pericardium. The annulus was stabilized by the endocardially implantable Bio-Ring Kalangos. Results. Intraoperative TEE showed a perfect repair of the tricuspid valve. The postoperative course was uneventful. The patient was treated with antibiotics as recommended for the next weeks. TTE seven days after the operation as well as 3 month follow up control did not show any recurrence of endocarditis or tricuspid insufficiency. Conclusions. Due to the special implantation technique, the Bio-Ring does not present any surface to the bloodstream. Therefore, after removal of all infected material, reinfections of the reconstructed valve should be very seldom. Papillary fibroelastoma of the aortic valvea case study During 2005-2007 6 newborns with atresia of small intestine proximal area have been operated in clinic. In all cases the disease manifested by clinical signs of high intestinal obstruction and accompanied with characteristic X-ray picture. Patients were transferred to our clinics 3-12 h after birth. Average gestational age of patients was 37 AE 0.2 weeks, average body weight 2980 AE 124 g. Atresia area was localized at 2-8 cm from the ligament of Treitz. In two cases direct anastomosis was made ''end-to-end''. In four cases the diameter of adductor loop considerably exceeded the diameter of efferent loop, and ''end-to-side'' anastomosis and jejunostomy were made. Due to jejunostomy more distally from the area of anastomosis a probe was placed through which feeding was done (2-3 days after the operation). After the beginning of enteral feeding of the child (5-6 days after) the probe was removed. In all cases jejunostomy was closed independently on the 18 th -22 nd day. No complications were noted in the post-operation period. All the patients survived. We consider that in the course of atresia of initial sections of small intestine, particularly in case of availability of a substantial gap in the diameter of proximal and distal segment of atretic intestine, T-shaped ''end-to-side'' anastomosis in combination with jejunostomy is considered to be justified. This enables to start feeding of patients early in the post-operation period, considerably facilitates the technique of operation as well as shortens the period of post-operational treatment of patients with such pathology. Background. Colonic atresia is a rare cause of congenital intestinal obstruction in the neonate. Methods. We reviewed complete records of 12 children treated for colonic atresia during the last 20-years period. Results. Six babies suffered from an isolated colonic atresia (group 1) and in other 6 cases (group 2) colonic atresia was either associated with additional intestinal atresias (n ¼ 2), or secondary to gastroschisis (n ¼ 4). Gestational age and birth weight were significantly lower in children from group 2 compared to group 1 (40 AE 0.5 v. 38 AE 0.7 wks [P < 0.05]; and 3600 AE 170 v. 2800 AE 200 g [P < 0.01], respectively). In 9 cases atresia was localized in the right colon, in 2 cases in colon transversum, and in one case in colon sigmoideum. The first surgical procedure was performed within 24 hrs after birth in all cases. Infants in group 1 received primary colostomies at the level of colonic atresia, followed by end-to-back anastomosis 4-6 weeks later. Four infants in group 2 needed ileo-coecal resection because of bowel necrosis and had a complicated post-operative period. Prior to final closure of the stoma in children from group 2 a Bishop-Koop anastomosis was placed. Mean hospital stay was 3.3 AE 0.4 wks in group 1 compared to 23 AE 6.9 wks in group 2 (P < 0.01). No children died in the group 1, whereas 2 children died in group 2 as the consequence of the extreme short bowel syndrome. Conclusions. Isolated colonic atresia is amenable with an excellent outcome. In contrast, infants with gastroschisis or other anomalies and associated colonic atresia may present a serious clinical challenge. Chirurgische Therapie eines nicht-chylösen Aszites -Fallbericht Background. Fat necrosis is thought to be a result of tissue ischemia, and its incidence after microsurgical free TRAM flap breast reconstruction has been reported anywhere from 3 to 26%. There is paucity on data on the effect of the recipient vessels on the rate of fat necrosis after free TRAM flap breast reconstruction. The purpose of this study was to evaluate the incidence of fat necrosis after unilateral, free TRAM flap breast reconstruction following anastomosis with the internal mammary vessels compared with the thoracodorsal artery and vein. Methods. Eight hundred and forty Consecutive patients who underwent unilateral, muscle-sparing free TRAM breast reconstruction from Memorial Sloan Kettering Cancer Center and the University of Los Angeles Medical Center were reviewed. Fat necrosis was defined as any postoperative firmness > 1cm, persisting > 3 months. Patients were matched for preoperative radiotherapy, obesity, smoking, diabetes mellitus, and prior abdominal surgery. Results. One hundred and seventeen reconstructions were performed at MSKCC using the internal mammary (IM) (n ¼ 49) or thoracodorsal (TD) (n ¼ 68) vessels. Thirty eight patients from each group were matched for the 5 above co-morbidities. 723 flaps were performed at UCLA using IM (n ¼ 60) or TD (n ¼ 663) vessels. 60 patients from each group were matched. Combining matched groups (n ¼ 98) yielded an incidence of 12, 24% and 29, 59% respectively (p ¼ 0.002). Conclusions. Based on the results of our series, it appears that the choice of recipient vessel can have a significant effect on the development of fat necrosis following free MS-TRAM flap breast reconstruction. Background. ''Clinical Pathways'' are a tool for process management in health care. Management of hernias is a common surgical problem, requiring a multidisciplinary process with complex interactions in the hospital (doctors -nurses -patient etc.). Methods. A professional ''process manager'' (together with a team of students) was invited to analyze the current clinical process of hernia management in our hospital. Different tools (questionnaires, interviews, etc.) were used to establish a ''clinical pathway''. Recommendations for improvement (e.g. stepwise introduction of day surgery) were suggested and subsequently implemented in clinical practice. Results. Altogether 397 patients undergoing hernia repair were evaluated (n ¼ 252 reference group=n ¼ 145 intervention group). A significant reduction of the length of hospital-stay was observed (total: 4.18 vs. 2.27 days; p < 0.0001; preoperative: 1.25 vs. 0.35; p < 0.0001; postoperative stay: 2.92 vs. 1.93; p < 0.0001). Standardization leads to a significant reduction of unnecessary diagnostic work-up (e.g. ultrasound examinations, X-ray in otherwise healthy individuals etc.; 1.85 vs. 1.05; p < 0.0001). Interestingly, a significant decrease of surgical complications achieved in the intervention group (1.85 vs. 1.05; p < 0.0001). Interviews with collaborators (nurses=surgeons) involved in the process of hernia treatment revealed a higher satisfaction regarding different items. The clinical process was subjectively estimated as markedly improved, although these results did not -presumably due to small sample size -reach statistical significance. Conclusions. Establishement of the ''Clinical Pathway'' for hernia management was found useful for improving the clinical process. Length of hospital stay, diagnostic work-up, complications as well as satisfaction of collaborators and patients could be improved. has become the standard procedure in therapy of primary or secondary peritonitis. The delayed closure of the abdominal wall after abdominal V.A.C. treatment is currently complicated due to the lateralisation of the edges of the fascia. We present early results of an innovative combination of techniques for the treatment of OA. Methods. Within the first surgical procedure using V.A.C.technique the fascia in the midline are approximated with a running suture of elastic vessel loop. At final closure the abdomen can be closed in the midline using a running nonresorbable suture. Results. We recorded no technique-specific complication. No incisional hernia occured until now. Conclusions. Sportsmen's hernia: What is the pathology found intraoperatively? Background. Sportsmen's hernia is a not well-defined entity of groin pain in sportsmen. Reports on Sportsmen's hernia include patients with ruptured muscle in the inguinal region, rupture of the falx inguinalis, a real medial or lateral hernia or widening of the inner inguinal ring. In many cases a not further defined bulge of the inguinal canal or no visible pathology at all is described. Methods. To investigate the pathology found during operation we reviewed the charts of all patients operated for Sportsmen's hernia between 2003 and 2007. Results. Twenty-five patients were identified with the diagnosis Sportsmen's hernia not responding to conservative treatment. All pat were football players. The pathology found intraoperatively was a widening of the inguinal canal of more than 2.5 cm in five patients. In not a single patient an inguinal canal lipoma or real medial or lateral hernia was found. There was no suspicion of rupture in the inguinal region. In all pat there was a typical bulge of the muscles in the triangle of Hesselbach. All but 3 patients were pain free and fit for training in an interval of three weeks after the operation. No patient suffered from the debilitating pain prior to the operation. Conclusions. There is no clear definition in the literature of what a sportsmen's hernia is. The operation for the so-called sportsmen's hernia can be very successfully even in cases were pre-or intraoperatively no clear pathology was found. Background. The use of perforating fixation devices has been identified as a leading cause of chronic pain in inguinal hernia repair. Therefore, a new implant design has been presented, combining a macroporous polypropylene mesh with a layer of slowly resorbing poly-lactid microhooks for ''self'' fixation (Progrip; PG; Covidien, Mansfield, USA). However, data on important outcome parameters, e.g. recurrences, seroma formation and postoperative pain (PP) is still scarce for the use of PG in Lichtenstein repair and formed the rationale to conduct this pilot trial. Methods. After having obtained informed written consent, nine non-selected consecutive patients with primary and recurrent (n ¼ 2) inguinal hernias (direct hernias, n ¼ 2; indirect, n ¼ 7) were operated by different surgeons in Lichtenstein technique with PG. These patients were observed for 12 months in order to elucidate recurrences, seroma formation and PP after the degradation of the hooks. Besides clinical examination, the visual analogue score (VAS) and the short form 36 health questionnaire were employed for the assessment of PP at subacute and chronic timepoints. Results. One early medial recurrence was observed after three months postoperatively. No clinically relevant seroma formation was detected within one year after surgery, whereas one wound infection occurred on the 2 nd postoperative day. A decrease of PP was assessed with the VAS and SF36, corresponding to high patient comfort. Conclusions. Based on the promising results we suggest the conduction of larger controlled trials on PG in Lichtenstein repair, especially emphasizing critical aspects (overlap) of its preshaped version. Background. Replication-competent herpes simplex type-1 viruses (HSV) selectively infect, replicate within, and lyse cancer cells. HSV therapy has been widely effective in multiple models of human malignancies. Noninvasive techniques would be valuable to predict the effectiveness of a specific therapy and spare costs and morbidity. The purpose of our study was to evaluate the impact of P-31 magnetic resonance spectroscopic imaging (MRSI) to predict the effectiveness of viral therapy in a human colon xenograft model. Methods. Five human colorectal cancer cell lines (C85, HCT8, HT29, LS147T, C18) were implanted s.c. in the flanks of nude mice. The in vivo tumor doubling times for each cell line were measured. Additionally, in vivo sensitivity of each tumor line to the replication-competent, attenuated herpes simplex type-1 oncolytic virus, NV1020 treatment was assessed. 1 Â 10 7 cells in 10 mice per cell line were implanted s.c. in the flanks. Palpable tumors of 5-7 mm in diameter were treated with 5 Â 10 6 plaque forming units of NV1020 or phosphate buffered saline by intratumoral injection. Tumor volumes were followed for 7 days. In a separate study group spectroscopic imaging was performed. The study consisted of T1weighted proton imaging for tumor localization followed by 1D-31P MRSI. Results. P-31 Spectra showed significant differences in the heights of PE and PC between virus sensitive and insensitive colon cancer lines. The PE=PC ratio correlated with both tumor doubling time and resistance to viral therapy. Conclusions. MR-Spectroscopy with resolution of PE and PC could be a useful, noninvasive predictor of sensitivity to oncolytic viral therapy. The carcinosarcoma of the liver is a very rare condition consisting of a mixture of carcinomatous and sarcomatous components. The incidence of this highly invasive and metastatic tumor entity reported in the literature is rare, with only few cases reported. Unlike the histological differences, the clinical aspect of the tumor is very similar to the ordinary liver cancer, including upper abdominal pain, weight loss and fatigue. We report a case of a 79-year-old male patient with a carcinosarcoma of the liver, who primary presented with abdominal pain in the left upper quadrant with weigh loss, abdominal fullness and dysphagia. Further evaluation revealed an extensive liver tumor of the left hepatic lobe with infiltration of the transverse colon. Histological examination of a punch biopsy taken from the tumor revealed a pleomorphic sarcoma. Subsequently, a resection of the left lateral liver segments was undertaken. The postoperative course was uneventful, and the patient was discharged after 30 days. Subsequently two weeks later the general condition of the patient deteriorated and the patient passed away. Histopathological examination showed a macroscopically nodular greyish white to greyish yellow solid tumor mass. The liver tissue was progressively infiltrated by epithelial tumor cells with phenotypic hepatocellular differentiation with intermingling pleomorphic bizarre spindle tumor cells. Based on the immunohistochemical analysis the tumor was identified as a carcinosarcoma of the liver. Vermeidung unerwarteter intraoperativer Befunde durch adäquate präoperative Diagnostik bei Patienten mit kolorektalen Lebermetastasen Background. TME is associated with a high anastomotic leakage rate. The aim of the study was to analyse which patients benefit from the creation of a protective ileostomy regarding all complications. Methods. One hundred and seventy nine patients who underwent TME with or without protective ileostomy out of 285 patients operated for rectal cancer between 1995 and 2005 were included in the study (other patients: abdominoperineal resection, palliative procedure). Following parameters were analyzed regarding postoperative complications: progression of cancer according to UICC-classification, tumor position, sex and age. Results. In 50 patients out of 179 with TME a protective ileostomy was created (28%); 50% (25 patients) received preoperative radiation therapy. Anastomotic leakage rate was 12% (6 patients, all men); in 4 of these patients relaparotomy (8%) was needed. Severe complications were higher in elder patients (67 vs. 63 yrs), other subgroups showed no difference. In the group without ileostomy (129 patients) 13 had anastomotic leakage (10.1%); in 11 of these patients relaparotomy was needed (8.5%), women (3.7%) and patients with tumor position above 12 cm (5%) had lower rate). Severe complications were higher in the subgroup of younger patients, men, progressed tumor stadium and low tumor position. Regarding all severe complications 19 patients (14.7%) were in the group without ileostomy vs. 8 patients (16%) with ileostomy; the subgroup with low tumor position benefit from ileostomy (14% vs. 22% relaparotomy rate). Minor complications were also higher in the group with ileostomy (42% vs. 22%). Conclusions. Protective Ileostomy could not reduce severe complications. Young patients, men, patients with low tumor position and patients with advanced tumor stage seem to benefit from protective ileostomy after TME. The relationship between previous elective PCI and the perioperative outcome after CABG remains undetermined. The aim of the study was to investigate whether patients referred for elective CABG after previous elective PCI have an increased perioperative risk. Methods. Between 01=2002 and 05=2007, 4412 consecutive patients underwent first-time open heart surgery at our department. After excluding patients with a history of emergent PCI, we isolated 306 patients with elective PCI during the last 24 months prior to CABG (Group 1) and compared them to 452 age-genderand EuroSCORE-matched patients without history of previous PCI, who underwent CABG during the same period (Group 2) in terms of perioperative mortality and complications and Major Adverse Cardiac Events (MACEs). Results. Both groups were comparable concerning preoperative EuroSCORE (Group 1: 4.83 AE 0.18, Group 2: 4.72 AE 0.14, p ¼ 0.63). This fact was associated with a worse logistic perioperative outcome (p ¼ 0.044). The incidence of bleeding complications (5.9% vs. 3.8%, p ¼ 0.017), the number of blood products (1.70 AE 0.31 vs. 0.61 AE 0.17, p < 0.001) used, as well as the incidence of acute renal failure (5.9% vs. 2.7%, p ¼ 0.025) and renal replacement therapy (3.6% vs. 1.7%, p ¼ 0.03) were higher in patients of the Group 1. Conclusions. Patients with previous elective PCI have a worse perioperative outcome in terms of mortality, MACE and perioperative complications. Durch diese Methode kann ein zumindest dauerhafteres Ergebnis, ohne Rezidiv, erreicht werden. The causes and pathogenesis of Dupuytren's disease (DD) are still unclear and very controversial. In principle, fibrotic changes develop as a consequence of four main types of primary events: (a) tissue destruction (e.g. liver cirrhosis); (b) inflammation (e.g. rheumatoid arthritis, arteriosclerosis); (c) contact with foreign body material (e.g. silicone implants); (d) spontaneous (e.g. DD). In the first three instances, it has been shown that significant numbers of mononuclear cells are present within the connective tissue mass that produce profibrotic cytokines. The present work is a first attempt to elucidate the possible mechanisms underlying ''spontaneous'' fibrotic diseases taking DD as a representative example. Surgically obtained tissue and blood samples of 100 DD patients were analysed by immunohistochemistry, flow cytometry, ELISA, immunoscope, tissue and cell culture techniques. The results are proof of massive infiltration by mononuclear cells (CD3þ, CD4> CD8, CD45RO > CD45RA, S100, CD56, CD68, few CD19, mast cells) forming dense perivascular clusters in DD. Fibromatosis derived T-cells showed a clear tendency to an oligonally resticted T-cell receptor repertoire, in contrast to the polyclonal pattern of autologous peripheral blood derived T-cells. Thus, it can be stated that inflammatory immunologic processes and a predominantely T-cell dependent and T-cell immune response could be involved in the pathogenesis of palmar fibromatosis. Ongoing studies aim at identifying the functional properties of these mononuclear cell subpopulations. This work is supported by the Lore-and Udo-Saldow Foundation, Medizinische Forschungs-Fonds Tirol (MFF) and Kompetenzzentrum Medizin Tirol (KMT Ergänzung. 3 Patienten der Gruppe offen hatten ein Doppelkarzinom, 1 Patient der Gruppe laparoskopisch war nicht zu werten, daher ergibt sich eine abweichende Gesamtzahl. In 2 of 3 cases an R2 resection was already recognized intraoperatively. Although follow-up is too short to make a definitive judgement (26.5 [15-37] months), survival seems to equal open surgery. Conclusions. In experienced hands and well-selected patients, laparoscopic colon resection is feasible, meets oncologic requirements and results in favourable results, which can easily compete with open surgery. In our experience this applies especially to all forms of laparoscopic rectal cancer surgery. First minimal invasive peritonectomy with intraperitoneal chemotherapy in a patient with pseudomyxoma peritonei Background. Pseudomyxoma peritonei (PMP) is a rare complication after rupture of an appendiceal mucocele and associated with pure prognosis in the absence of cytoreductive therapy. Combined peritonectomy with hyperthermic intraperitoneal chemotherapy favours the outcome, however this procedure is associated with substantial postoperative morbidity. We describe the first case of minimally invasive peritonectomy with combined intraoperative hyperthermic chemotherapy in a patient with PMP. Methods. A 21-year-old woman underwent diagnostic laparoscopy due to aggravating lower abdominal pain. A perforated appendix, mucous masses in the Douglas space and miliar lesions in the parietal peritoneum, arousing suspicion for PMP, were found. Histology revealed a benign mucinous tumor of the appendix and confirmed PMP in biopsies taken from the peritoneum. 10 days after appendectomy, laparoscopic peritonectomy and intraoperative hyperthermic chemotherapy with mitomycin C (30 mg=m 2 ) have been carried out. Results. Due to a restricted tumor spreading onto the parietal right hemiperitoneum no organ resection was necessary. Laparoscopic peritonectomy and intraperitoneal hyperthermic chemotherapy by use of a closed cycle perfusion system was carried out successfully. The procedure was well tolerated by the patient, neither intra-nor postoperative complications occurred. She was dismissed on postoperative day eight in an excellent condition. Conclusions. We here describe the worldwide first case of a laparoscopic peritonectomy with a combined intraoperative intraperitoneal hyperthermic chemotherapy in a patient with PMP. The minimally invasive approach resulted in a good cosmetic result and rapid recovery of the patient and should be considered as a therapeutic option in patients with PMP and limited spreading. Background. Laparoscopic liver resection is nowadays considered for surgical treatment of hepatic malignancies. We developed a novel interdisciplinary approach using navigated radiofrequency ablation (RFA) to guide minimal invasive liver resection to increase procedural safety in patients with limited parenchymal hepatic mass. Methods. We report on two patients suffering from multiple bilateral liver metastases. Patients were bedded on a body fixation device and received CT acquisition, 3D-planning of possible resection planes and central metastases, navigation, targeting, needle placement in apnea and synchronous thermal ablation. Thereafter laparoscopic liver resection was carried out respecting the preformed necrotic planes. Results. All procedures were completed laparoscopically. Navigated thermal ablations of the resection planes were successfully carried out to guide resection of segments II, III, IVa in both patients. Laparoscopic atypical resections (metastasectomies) were performed to remove tumors in segments VI and VII. Metastases in segments V and VIII were treated by means of navigated RFA. Determined blood loss was 50 ml and 250 ml. Incisions for specimen removal yielded 7 cm. No complication occurred. Patients were discharged on day 7 and 8, respectively. Conclusions. This novel approach allows safe parenchyma sparing laparoscopic liver resections. The benefits of minimally invasive liver surgery countervail against higher procedural demands. Laparoscopic liver resection compared to navigated RFA-guided liver resection in a porcine model Background. Laparoscopy has become more important in the surgical treatment of liver diseases. Since technical devices are by far not optimized yet we evaluated a novel approach for minimal invasive liver resection in an animal model. Methods. Twelve housepigs were enrolled in this study for left-lobe liver resection. Six animals (Group 1) were bedded on a body fixation device and received CT acquisition, 3D-planning of resection plane, navigation, targeting, needle placement in apnea and synchronous thermal ablation. Thereafter resection was carried out laparoscopically. Six animals (Group 2) underwent laparoscopic liver resection using bipolar energy sources, staplers and clips. Animals were sacrificed after the procedure. Procedural parameters, thermal necrosis and serum markers (CRP, IL-6, LFP) were assessed. Results. All but one procedures were completed laparoscopically. One conversion (Group 2) was carried out to manage bleeding from the left hepatic vein. Mean blood loss yielded 16 ml in Group 1 and 92 ml in Group 2 (p ¼ 0.001). No bile leak was observed. Navigated RFA sufficiently prepared resection plane in Group 1 animals (no staplers in Group 1 compared to 4 staplers=procedure in Group 2). Overall procedural time was 93 min (Group 1) and 34 min (Group 2, p ¼ 0.001). Time for laparoscopic resection was not different between both groups. Histology revealed necrotic margins of 9 mm and 2 mm in Group 1 and 2, respectively. Serum marker profiles were not significantly different in both groups. Conclusions. This novel approach of navigated RFA-guided laparoscopic liver resection allows accurate preparation of the resection plane adding operative safety, reducing blood loss and the need for staplers. Das Background. With the widespread availability and use of maternal ultrasonography, the incidence of urinary tract disorders diagnosed in utero has increased substantially. But it is well accepted that urinary tract dilatation does not always indicate the need of treatment. On the other hand there are patients presenting severe urinary tract infection due to a urinary disorder, which has not been antenatally diagnosed. Methods. We analysed the records of all children under the first year of life (n ¼ 194) at our institution who underwent evaluation for hydronephrosis. The cause of hydronephrosis, the existence of antenatal detection, complications, renal impairment and the mode of treatment were retrospectively reviewed. All neonates with hydronephrosis achieved low-dose antibiotic therapy till the clarification of cause was completed. Nuclear scan has been performed to evaluate renal function. Seventy five percent of our patients were antenatally diagnosed, whereas 25% presented acute abdominal pain and urinary tract infection during the first year of life. Pheochromocytoma in children: personal experience Medical University, Lviv, Uktraine, Lviv, Ukraine Pheocromocytoma is one of the causes of arterial hypertension in children. Attempts to treat the arterial hypertension without clear establishing of its etiology lead to the development serious changes in cardiovascular system with the high risk of lethality. This study summarized results of treatment of 9 children with pheochromocytoma. The mean age was 12.3 AE 2.1. The urinary metanephrine level, ultrasonography and CT were applied for the diagnosis of pheochromocytoma. Extraadrenal localization of tumor was in one patient. The unilateral localization of pheochromocytoma was in 8 patients. All patients were operated: in 7 (77.8%) patients conventional adrenalectomy was performed and in 2 (22.2%) -laparoscopic adrenalectomy. Eight (88.9%) patients had persistent form of hypertension and one (11.1%) patient was normotensive. Except of arterial hypertension, headache (77.8%), palpitation (66.7%), and polyuria (44.4%) were the common symptoms of pheochromocytoma. The hypertensive retinopathy and cardiomyopathy was noted in 2 patients. The elevated level of urinary metanephrine was noted in 8 patients (28.37-59.24 mg=24 h) and in case of normotensive pheochromocytoma this test had a normal value (5.72 mg=24 h). Despite the medication, the intraoperative hypertension was noted in 3 patients that required the infusion of sodium nitroprusside. The conventional adrenalectomy was performed through lumbotomy in 6 patients and in one patient with the extraadrenal localization of pheochromocytoma -through transabdominal approach. The laparoscopic adrenalectomy was performed through retroperitoneal approach. The duration of conventional and laparoscopic adrenalectomy had no significant differences. Pathologic features suggestive of benign character of tumor were noted in all patients. Grundlagen. Die Rezidivhäufigkeit nach Fundoplikatio ist signifikant höher, wenn die Operation bei kataboler Stoffwechsellage durchgeführt wird. Ziel der prospektiven Studie ist die Identifizierung möglicher Laborparameter zum Monitoring der präoperativen Stoffwechsellage. Methodik. Seit 2003 wurde bei insgesamt 12 dystrophen Reflux-Patienten (1-42a, Ø 17a, BMI unter der 10. Perzentile) vor der geplanten Fundoplikatio eine Stoffwechselabklärung hinsichtlich folgender Laborparamenter durchgefü hrt: Präalbumin, Cholinesterase (CHE), Zink, Laktat, TNF-Alpha, CRP und Transferrin wurden in wöchentlichem Abstand präoperativ und bis zu 24 Wochen postoperativ bestimmt. Weiters wurden der Body-Mass-Index (BMI) und die Kalorienaufnahme sowohl enteral als auch parenteral dokumentiert. Der Energiequotient der Patienten wurde durch Anpassung der Nahrungszufuhr optimiert. Die Fundoplikatio erfolgte bei Normalisierung des Präalbuminwertes. Prä-und postoperativ wurde die Refluxdiagnostik mittels pH-Metrie, Ö sophaguspassage sowie endoskopischen Biopsien komplettiert. Ergebnisse. Präalbumin, CHE und Transferrin reagierten durch konstanten Anstieg rasch auf die gesteigerte Energiezufuhr und erwiesen sich als empfindlichste Marker zur Monitorisierung der Stoffwechsellage. Zink, Laktat, TNF-Alpha und CRP waren wie auch der BMI nicht entsprechend aussagekräftig, da sie nicht in allen Fällen mit der Stoffwechsellage korrelierten. Zehn der inkludierten Patienten wurden fundopliziert, wobei bisher keine Rezidive auftraten. Bei zwei weiteren Patienten besserte sich der Ernährungszustand signifikant, so dass die Eltern eine Antirefluxplastik vorerst ablehnen. Schlussfolgerungen. Ösophago-gastrale Dissoziation bei ausgeprägtem gastro-ösophagealem Reflux (GÖR) bei tetraspastischen Kinderneine Alternative zur konventionellen Fundoplikatio Landes-, Frauen-und Kinderklinik, Linz, Österreich Grundlagen. Die Fundoplikatio ist der Standardeingriff bei Kindern mit GÖ R, bei denen die konservative Therapie nicht zum Erfolg führt. Bei Kindern mit zusätzlichen Fehlbildungen, besonders bei tetraspastischen Kindern, ist mit einer hohen Rezidivrate (12-45%) zu rechnen. Bianchi beschrieb 1997 erstmals die ösophago-gastrale Dissoziation als Alternativeingriff zur Fundoplikatio. Damit ist es möglich, dass langfristig kein Rezidiv entstehen kann und die Patienten von Seiten des Refluxes beschwerdefrei bleiben. Methodik. Die Indikation zur Operation wird nach entsprechender Diagnosesicherung durch ein Magenröntgen, einer histologischen Verifizierung der Refluxkrankheit im Rahmen einer Gastroskopie und evt. einer pH-metrie gestellt. Die Operation beginnt mit der Darstellung des gastro-ösophagealen Ü berganges wie zu einer Fundoplikatio. Anschließend wird das Jejunum 35 cm nach der Treitz'schen Flexur durchtrennt und der distale Schenkel retrocolisch an den Ö sophagus gebracht. Nach Absetzen des Magens vom Ö sophagus wird die Cardia verschlossen. Nun erfolgt die ösophago -jejunale End-zu-Seit-Anastomose. Im Anschluss an die Fußpunktanastomose wird bei Verdacht auf eine Magenentleerungsstörung eine Pyloroplastik durchgeführt und abschließend eine Gastrostomie für die Ernährung mit einem Gastrotube angelegt. Ergebnisse. Im Zeitraum vom März 2006 bis zum Oktober 2007 haben wir 3 tetraspastische Kinder mit schwerem gastroösophagealem Reflux operiert. Zwei Kinder waren 9 Jahre, eines 17 Jahre alt. Bei allen drei Kindern wurde der GÖ R radiologisch und histologisch verifiziert. Ein Kind hatte bereits vor der Operation eine PEG-Sonde, ein weiteres eine jejunale Sonde über eine PEG. Alle Kinder hatten in der Anamnese rezidivierende Aspirationspneumonien. Bei allen Kindern war der perioperative Verlauf problemlos. Ein Kind hatte eine Wundheilungsstörung, diese heilte aber spontan ab. Zwei Kinder sind jetzt 8 bzw. 22 Monate nach der Operation beschwerdefrei und die Pflege daheim ist problemlos. Beide Kinder nehmen adäquat an Gewicht zu. Das dritte Kind verstarb 1 Woche nach dem Eingriff nach anfänglicher Besserung an einem zentralen therapierefraktären Fieber ohne direkten Zusammenhang mit der Operation. Dies wurde auch in der Obduktion bestätigt. Schlussfolgerungen. Die ösophago-gastrale Dissoziationsoperation stellt bei einem GÖ R bei tetraspastischen Kindern eine gute Alternative zur Fundoplikatio dar. Sie ist technisch aufwendiger, demgegenüber profitieren die Patienten aber dadurch, dass der Reflux und seine Symptome beinahe immer (99%) sistieren. Auch langfristig ist mit keinem Rezidiv zu rechnen. Als Indikation sehe ich tetraspastische Patienten mit GÖ R, die wegen einer schlechten Nahrungsaufnahme eine PEG-Sonde benötigen oder bereits haben und Patienten mit schweren anatomischen Veränderungen im Cardia-und Hiatusbereich. Ein wichtiges Ziel bei diesen Kindern ist eine problemlose Sondenernährung ohne Refluxsymptomatik und eine entsprechender Gewichtszunahme. Ergebnisse. Die Fläche der Portalfelder nahm signifikant zu und ebenso die Anzahl der Hepatozyten in den Portalfeldern. Analysis of molecular markers of lymphozyte migration in human hand allografts: relevance in skin rejection Background. To understand in greater depth the molecular mechanisms involved in skin rejection in hand transplantation, we investigated 8 key molecular markers of lymphocyte trafficking, cellular rejection and antibody mediated rejection in human hand transplant biopsies. Methods. One hundred and four skin biopsies taken from three bilateral hand transplants were assessed by H & E histology (graded 0-4b) and immunohistochemistry using antibodies for: Antigen (HLA)-II (DP,DQ,DR), Psoriasin ¼ S100A7 and C4d. Levels of expression were assessed (0, þ,þ þ,þ þ þ) and read in the light correlated with rejection as well as time after transplantation. Results. Rejection ranged between grade 0 and 4a with an average score of 0.94. In healthy skin, none of the markers was consistently up-regulated. Upon rejection, CD54, CD62E and CD62P staining in endothelial cells was significantly increased. Expression of CD62E and CD62P correlated well with severity of rejection. The majority of infiltrating lymphocytes stained positive for CD11a. CD144 was detected on endothelial cells, but its occurrence did not correlate with rejection. Psoriasin expression was observed in keratinocytes in a basal and focal pattern and correlated well with rejection. For C4d, no consistent staining pattern was observed indicating that antibody mediated rejection did not play a role in these patients. Strong evidence towards higher expression of all markers at later time-points after transplantation was found. Conclusions. Molecular markers involved in lymphocyte trafficking are up-regulated upon skin rejection after hand transplantation and represent promising target for prophylaxis and treatment of rejection in Composite Tissue Allotransplantation. Survival signaling by C-RAF: mitochondrial ROS and Ca 2þ are critical targets A. Kuznetsov 1;2 , J. Smiegelskaite 1;2 , C. Doblander 1;2 , M. Janakiraman 1;2 , M. Hermann 3;2 , M. Wurm 3;2 , R. Sucher 1;2 , J. Troppmair 1;2 RAF kinases feature prominently in human tumor development through mutations in RAF proteins themselves as well as in upstream components. Activated RAF contributes to transformation through enhanced cell cycle progression and prevention of apoptotic cell death. Survival signaling by RAF occurs through largely unknown mechanisms resulting in the maintenance of mitochondrial integrity. Here we provide evidence for the first time that RAF controls cell survival by maintaining permissive levels of mitochondrial reactive oxygen species (ROS) and Ca 2þ . IL-3 withdrawal from 32D cells resulted in ROS production, which was suppressed by activated C-RAF. C-RAF also delayed the onset of apoptosis, following treatment with staurosporine (STS) or the oxidative stress-inducing agent tert-butyl hydroperoxide (t-BHP). Apoptotic cell death is preceded by a ROS-dependent increase in mitochondrial Ca 2þ , which was absent in cells expressing transforming C-RAF. Prevention of mitochondrial Ca 2þ overload after IL-3 deprivation delayed apoptotic cell death. In summary, our data show that survival control by C-RAF involves controlling ROS production, which otherwise perturbs mitochondrial Ca 2þ homeostasis. MAPK signaling during ischemia and reperfusion: stress kinase regulation of mitochondrial ROS and Ca 2þ homeostasis P. Gehwolf 1;2 , R. Sucher 1;2 , T. Kaier 1;2 , M. Maglione 1;2 , S. Schneeberger 1;2 , G. Brandacher 1;2 , R. Öllinger 1;2 , M. Hermann 3;2 , A. Krutznetzov 1;2 , C. Margreiter 1;2 , H. Weiss 1;2 , R. Margreiter 1;2 , J. Troppmair 1;2 Ischemia (I) and reperfusion (R) trigger a series of events, which culminate in severe injuries to transplanted organs. Reactive oxygen species (ROS) have long been implicated in IR-associated tissue injury (IRI) through effects on pro-apoptotic signaling, mitochondrial function and intracellular Ca 2þ trafficking leading mitochondrial dysfunction and cell death. Intracellular signaling pathways also respond to other cellular changes occurring during I=R and modulate the extent of damage. Using the cardiomyocyte cell line HL-1, primary fetal cardiomyocytes and a heterotopic murine heart transplant model, MAPK activation was assessed in vitro and in vivo. Here we demonstrate that 45 min of ischemia=hypoxia primarily caused the activation of stress kinases p38 and JNK, reoxygenation resulted in a dramatic and almost synchronous increase in ERK, JNK, and p38 activity in vitro as well as in vivo. Stress kinase activity returned to basal levels while ERK1, 2 still were active by the end of the observation period (48 h). Hypoxia also lead to a dramatic increase in mitochondrial ROS production, Ca 2þ levels and apoptosis, which were prevented in the presence of anti-oxidant N-acetyl cysteine (NAC). Background. The current shortage of organ donors has led many centers to use marginal and nonheart-beating donors. Recent research has implicated the infiltration of leukocytes as an important mediator of ischemia-reperfusion injury (IRI). The fibrin derived peptide B15-42 reduces leukocyte infiltration by inhibiting the transmigration process. In cardiac transplantation and myocardial infarction models it could have been shown that B15-42 reduces IRI in the heart. Now we wanted to test the effects of the peptide on renal ischemia reperfusion injury. Methods. Male Lewis rats (250-300 g) underwent median laparotomy with removal of the right kidney, followed by clamping of the left renal artery for 60-min. Groups were dived into follow up periods of 24-hours and 7-days, each group was further dived into a control group (IRI only) and a treatment group IRI þ B15-42 (1.2 mg i.v.). Serum samples for the evaluation of creatinine and BUN levels were collected at several time points. Results. Over the reperfusion period we could observe, that 60-min of ischemia led to increasing Creatinine and BUN levels in the ischemia only group with a peak at day 2. After day 2 renal function recovers and reaches normal levels on day 7 again. The application of B15-42 led to a reduction of Creatinine and BUN levels, which was significant on day 2 and day 5. In animals receiving B15-42 we could measure normal creatinine and BUN levels over the whole reperfusion periode. Conclusions. Our experiments show that B15-42 is not only a possible agent for cardiac but also for renal ischemia-reperfusion injury.
