Hammer 1 , K. Prein 2 , W. Bruenner 1 , C. Bauer 1 , S. Lax 2 , P. Steindorfer 1 Grundlagen. Die Sentinel-Lymphknoten (SLN)-Biopsie ist eine weithin anerkannte Methode des axillären Stagings beim invasiven Mamma-Carcinom (IMC). Gemäß St.Gallen-Consensus sowie den aus NSABP-B27 abzuleitenden Daten werden diesbezü gliche kombinierte Detektionsmethoden des SLN mittels Radionuklid-und Blaumarkierung an unserer Abteilung angewandt. Ziel. Die Analyse der Auffindungsrate des axillären SLN beim IMC durch die kombinierte Detektionsmethode mittels Gammasonde bei Radionuklidmarkierung sowie Blaumarkierung in unserem Patientenkollektiv. Methodik. 132 Patienten mit cN-0 sowie IMC < 30 mm, präoperativ mittels Feinnadelbiopsie diagnostiziert, wurden inkludiert. Lymphatisches ,,Mapping'' zur Darstellung des SLN erfolgte durch subareoläre oder peritumorale Injektion von Tc99-markiertem Albumin sowie PatentblauV, gefolgt von der Detektion mittels Gammasonde und intraoperativer Visualisierung blaugefärbter Lymphknoten. Jeder SLN (definiert durch Blaufärbung oder positiver Nuklid-Aktivität) wurde mittels Gefrierschnitt, Stufenserienschnitten nach Standardprotokoll sowie Cytokeratin-Immunohistochemie aufgearbeitet. Ergebnisse. Bei 132 Patienten (mit insgesamt 294 untersuchten SLN) fanden sich 50 Patienten (38%) mit Tumorzel-len im SLN, von denen 16 (12%) nur immunhistochemisch nachgewiesen wurden. Bei 20 Patienten (15%) war die Darstellung des SLN zwischen beiden Detektions-Methoden diskrepant. In 2 Fällen (1,5%) detektierte sich der SLN nur ü ber die Färbung, beide jeweils nodalpositiv, 18 Patienten (13,5%) zeigten einen SLN mit ausschließlicher Gammasondenaktivität ohne Blaufärbung, davon 9 Patienten (7%) mit Tumorzellen im SLN. In Summe wiesen somit 11 (8,5%) der 20 diskrepanten Fälle Tumorzellbefall im SLN auf. Schlussfolgerungen. Durch die alleinige Verwendung nur einer Markierungs-Methode kann es zur fehlenden Auffindung etwaiger tumorzellbefallener SLN kommen (in 8,5% unseres Patientenkollektivs). Das kombinierte Markierungsverfahren mittels Nuklid-und Blauapplikation erscheint bevorzugt zu verwenden zu sein, um eine korrekte SLN-Detektion zu erzielen. Perioperative chemotherapy at local advanced breast cancer-prostpective study from 1987 to 2007 A. Heiss, F. Kober, M. Hermann The local advanced breast cancer has five year survival rate of 0%, a relapse rate of 50% (Haagensen and Stout. Ann Surg 1943) with surgical intervention only. In the last years the perioperativ chemotherapy is installed increasingly with great success on local advanced breast cancer. According to different statements in literature an improvement of survival rate to over more than 50% will be reached. Within the scope of a prospective study 54 patients from our collection of clinical cases had a perioperative chemotherapy. All patients of these clinical cases could be evaluated. Thirty nine patients were post menopausal, 9 patients pre menopausal and on 6 patients the hormone status was unknown. The inclusion criterions were stages T3, T4 N0-N3, M0-M1, T2, N pos., M0-M1. We had 27 patients with stage T4 and 13 patients had referred metastasis. Thirteen patients had exulceration carcinoma, 7 an inflammatory and 26 patients had a carcinoma, which was not movable towards thorax wall. The patients received the perioperativ chemotherapy under the CNF schema (Endoxan, 5-FU and Novantron). Results. We had on 8 Patients a complete response. The 3year survival rate was 77%, the 5 and 10-year survival rate was 62%. Methods. Four-hundred and sixty-seven consecutive liver transplants (LTs) performed between 1998 and 2001 in 402 patients were analyzed in a longitudinal cohort study. Results. A total of 77 patients in this cohort developed 198 de novo malignancies. Of the 51 patients with skin cancer, seven were additionally diagnosed with non skin cancer and the total number of skin cancer lesions that were identified was 163. Twenty-four patients had multiple skin cancers. There were 6 patients who had 6 melanomas removed, 29 patients who had 57 basal cell carcinomas removed, and 34 patients with 100 squamous cell cancers removed. The mean age at the first diagnosis of skin cancer was 59 years. Mean time from LT to skin cancer diagnosis was 35 months. Eight patients had had skin cancer prior to transplantation with an average time to onset of cancer after transplantation of 28 months. Patient suffering from HCV who received interferon therapy had a significantly decreased incidence of skin cancer. Conclusions. We present the largest series of LT recipients using TAC based immunosuppression with skin cancer to date. Squamous cell cancer is the most common form of skin cancer in our cohort and a more rapid development of skin cancer from time of LT than previously reported data was found. IFN therapy or recurrent hepatitis C may have a protective effect against the development of skin cancer. Hauptthema -Qualitätssicherung P020 Die Psyche des Chirurgenein Risikofaktor? Während manuelles Können und Erfahrung des Chirurgen als mögliche Risikofaktoren identifiziert worden sind, ist die Psyche des Chirurgen bisher nicht Gegenstand dieser Analysen gewesen. Es gibt aber definierte psychische settings, die regelmäßig auftreten und besonders risikoträchtig sind. Die erste dieser Stationen ist der Ü bergang vom Assistenten zum selbstständigen Operateur, in der Phase wo die Hybris soweit geht, dass der Chirurg meint, quasi ,,vom Blatt spielen'' zu können. Nächstes Szenario ist die Komplikation nach einer Routine-Operation, die dann einen fatalen Verlauf nimmt. Und drittes setting ist die Operation, die der Chirurg in Ü berschätzung des eigenen Könnens und bisweilen auch der Möglichkeiten seines Umfeldes, ü bernimmt. Wie können solche Situationen präventiert werden? Einfachste Möglichkeit wäre, nur Chirurgen einzustellen, die über eine ausreichende Selbstreflektion verfügen. Aber einerseits ist die prognostische Beurteilung schwierig, und andererseits setzt Chirurgie ein gewisses Maß an Selbstüberzeugung voraus. Daher sollten während der Facharztausbildung nicht nur fachliche und OP-technische Aspekte vermittelt werden, sondern auch psychische Be-und Verarbeitungsstrukturen. Wer eine gelungene Operation als persönlichen Triumph feiert, wird misslungene Operationen als persönliche Niederlagen erleben. Geht man eine Operation jedoch nach bestem Wissen und Gewissen an, so ist das Endergebnis deutlich weniger emotional behaftetim positiven und im negativen Fall. Letzte Präventionsmöglichkeit sind externe Ü berwachungsmaßnahmen wie Visiten, Fall-Konferenzen und im besten Fall ein ärztlicher Supervisor, der nicht selbst in die Patientenversorgung eingebunden ist. Background. One of principal causes of lethality of patients with severe acute pancreatitis is multiorgan dysfunction. Multiorgan failure often associates with presence of ascites and parapancreatic exudates. Methods. We studied 76 patients with severe acute pancreatitis. We measured interleukins 1, 6, 8, 18, in ascitic liquid and blood serum. Evacuation of ascitic fluid used in 40 patients, others served as control group. Results. In admission concentration of all interleukins and adhesion molecules was higher in PAFC, than serum. Evacuation of ascites improved the general condition of patients. In control group show gradual rising levels of proinflammatory mediators within a week that correlated with the advance organ dysfunctions. Levels of circulating mediators decreased already next day after evacuation of PAFC in basic group patients, function of organs improved. After removed of ascites the number of patients, which the open surgical interventions were spent, has considerably decreased. After evacuation of PAFC function of kidneys and a liver much more quickly improved, the pulmonary complications decreased. Conclusions. In complex management of acute necrotizing pancreatitis we include evacuation of PAFC. It considerably improves function of lungs, kidneys and liver, reduces risk of infected necroses. Background. We report our experiences with management of severe blunt abdominal trauma with liver involvment. Methods. Retrospective review of all patients with blunt liver trauma requiring intensive care unit admittance at our institution between 01=2000 and 04=2007. Liver trauma was graded according to the Organ Injury Scale (American Association for the Surgery of Trauma). Data are reported as total numbers (%) or mean AE standard deviation. Results. A total of 159 patients (35.2% female, mean age 34.22 AE 17.76 years) were included. Pattern of accident included traffic (56.0%), sport (17.6%), fall (21.4%), and others (5.0%). Liver trauma was grade I in 14.5%, grade II in 19.5%, grade III in 52.8%, grade IV in 12.58% and grade V in 0.6%. Six isolated liver traumas (2 Â grade III, 4 Â grade IV) occured, while 98.1% of patients were polytraumatized, and 28.3% had concomitant splenic injury. Surgery was necessary in 33 patients (20.76%), with 18 patients (11.32%) undergoing hepatic surgery. Mortality was 11.32%, with no death directly related to the hepatic or splenic trauma. On univariate analysis, predictors of mortality were hemodynamic instability during transportation to hospital (p ¼ 0.009), or upon hospital admittance (p ¼ 0.0001), pulmonary complications (p ¼ 0.014) or infections (p ¼ 0.004) post-trauma, and hemodynamic instability on post-trauma day 1 (p ¼ 0.016) and day 2 (p ¼ 0.018), but not degree of liver trauma (p ¼ 0.733) or surgical intervention (p ¼ 0.139). Conclusions. In this cohort of polytraumatized patients, 88.68% of the liver traumas could be managed non-operatively. Mortaliy was not related to the degree of liver trauma, or need for surgery. Postoperative morbidity of pancreatic head resection for chronic pancreatitis Background. Pancreatic head resection for chronic pancreatitis is indicated for therapy-resistant chronic pain, or when malignancy is suspected. Methods. Retrospective review of all consecutive pancreatic head resections performed for pancreatitis at our institution between 01=2003 and 01=2007. Data are reported as total numbers (%) or mean AE standard deviation. Results. Twenty-three patients (30.4% females) with a mean age of 52.8 AE 11.7 years underwent Whipple procedure (WP) (13 patients, 56.5%), or duodenum-preserving pancreatic head resection (DPPHR) (10 patients, 43.5%). Seventeen patients (73.9%) reported previous pancreatitis, and malignancy was suspected in 9 (39.1%). Length of stay was 22.2 AE 13.21 days, with 6 patients (26.1%) requiring ICU care for 9.2 AE 11.7 days. Postoperative morbidity was 39.1% (9 patients), including pulmonary complications in 8.7%, hemorhage in 8.7%, intraabdominal abscess in 4.3%, and pancreatic anastomosis leakage in 21.8% (WP 15.4% vs. DPPHR 30.0%, p ¼ 0.367). Four patients (17.4%) underwent recurrent surgery 5.8 AE 3.3 days after resection (WP 0 vs. DPPHR 4, p ¼ 0.024). Late complications included 2 incisional hernias (8.7%), one requiring surgical repair. Procedure related mortality was 0%, and one patient died 33 months after WP of leukemia. After a mean follow-up of 21.9 AE 16.1 months, 4 patients (17.4%) had been readmitted for pancreas related complications. Conclusions: In this cohort, malignancy was suspected in almost 40% of patients, resulting in a high number of Whipple procedures. With no postoperative mortality, anastomotic complication rate was high, especially in the DPPHR group. Background. Liver abscess is a rare complication after pancreatectomy. Clostridium perfingens is a rare cause of intrahepatic infections. Case report. A 65-year-old woman was diagnosed with pancreatic cancer with infiltration of the hepatic artery. Neoadjuvant radiochemotherapy with capecitabine was started, which caused tumour regression and duodenopancreatectomy was performed. The portal vein was found to be occluded and infiltrated by cancer and therefore, was ligated. After a slow recovery, the patient developed a hemorrhage at the gastrojejunal anastomosis, which was controlled by fibrin injection. Within few days she presented with signs of sepsis and blood cultures grew Clostridium perfringens, Streptococcus oralis, Staphylococcus aureus and Candida albicans. The source of the sepsis was found to be a 10cm liver abscess, which was percutaneously drained; cultures grew Clostridium perfringens, Hafnia alvei and Enterobacter cloacae. Despite antibiotic treatment the patient deteriorated and died 27 days after pancreatic surgery from sepsis and multiorgan failure. Conclusions. Such rare infections must be considered after pancreatic resection with neoadjuvant chemotherapy. Clostridium perfringens liver abscess remains to be associated with a high mortality rate. Skeletal muscle protein catabolism is influenced by short-term neuromuscular electrical stimulation: a prospective, randomized, controlled, single-blind trial in major abdominal surgery patients Background. Skeletal muscle atrophy is associated with catabolic conditions such as sepsis, trauma, burns, aging or major surgical interventions and leads to reduced muscle strength, increased clinical complications and prolonged convalescence. Recently several studies revealed postoperative immobilisation as a major risk factor for muscle wasting in severely ill patients. This study has been conducted to investigate the potency of neuromuscular electrical stimulation on muscle metabolism during the first four postoperative days after major abdominal surgery. Study design: prospective, randomized, controlled, singleblind clinical trial. Methods. One leg of the patients was treated with NMES for 4 days starting on the first postoperative day. The other leg was used as sham stimulated control. In total muscle biopsies of both legs of 18 patients were gained after the last stimulation. Results. NMES significantly increased total RNA content ( þ 26%) and total sarcoplasmatic protein content ( þ 20%) but has no effect on myofibrillar protein content. Similarly, NMES reduced ubiquitin-conjugated sarcoplasmatic proteins (À 23%) and proteasome activity ( À 34%) but did not influence ubiquitin conjugation of myofibrillar proteins. The mechano growth factor mRNA level correlated positively with the applied current and negatively with the body mass index of the patients. The IGF-1Ea mRNA level increase after NMES correlated negatively with the age of the patients. Conclusions. This study shows that short term NMES activates muscle protein translational capacity and reduces parameters of sarcoplasmatic protein degradation in catabolic surgical patients. Therefore NMES is a useful clinical tool to treat protein catabolism in surgical patients. Background. The study analyses 100 consecutive cases of FNACs regarding to its reliability on the indication of surgery and intraoperative strategies. Methods. Based on the cytological results the FNACs were divided in adequate and inadequate FNACs. The adequate FNACs were further subdivided in FNACs without suspicion of malignancy, FNACs with suspicion of malignancy and FNACs with proofed malignancy. After the surgery these cytological results were compared with the postoperative histological results. Results. The inadequacy rate was 30%. Postoperative we detected 4 malignant cases (13%), 12 cases with increased risk of malignancy (40%) and 14 benignant cases in this group (47%). The adequacy rate was 70%. This group contains 21 cases without suspicion of malignancy (30%), 45 cases with suspicion of malignancy (64%) and 4 cases with proofed malignancy (6%). The histological reprocessing showed 29 benignant cases, 20 cases with increased risk of malignancy and 21 malignant cases. The outcome of comparing the cytological with the histological results was: Cases without suspicion of malignancy (30%) were ratified in 71%. Certainly in 29% a neoplasia was detected in spite of a benignant cytological result. Cases with suspicion of malignancy (64%) turned out to be a neoplasia in 69%. Cases with proofed malignancy (6%) corresponded in all cases (100%). Conclusions. The FNAC underlines an indication of surgery. It has to be considered that the proof or exclusion of malignancy is only in71% correct, in comparison to histology. Dreifach-Pathologie der Appendix Background. The treatment standard for early esophageal adenocarcinoma -radical esophagectomy -is currently challenged. Interventional endoscopists propagate fragmented resections of neoplastic mucosa (EMR). Surgeons doubt the oncologic adequacy of this concept, but agree that limited surgery may be justified. Methods. A literature review was performed and ten major reasons were identified, supporting adequacy of a limited surgical resection and reconstruction with a pedicled jejunal segment ('Modified Merendino Procedure'). Results. 1) Local tumor spread is rather limited in most cases. 2) Multifocal tumour growth within the precancerous Barrett mucosa can be adequately approached with resection of the entire metaplastic epithelium. 3) Depth of invasion -which can only be defined with low accuracy preoperatively -does not matter, when the full thickness of the esophageal wall is resected. 4) Lymphatic spead occurs predominantly in the immediate anatomical region of the primary tumor and 'skip metastases' are extremely rare. Lymphadenectomy with the limited procedure is adequate. 5) Complete (''R0'') resections can be achieved with high likelihood. 6) The predisposing disorder, i.e. ''gastroesophageal reflux'' can be reliably eliminated with jejunal interposition (''Merendino''). 7) Psychooncology: Patients show good mental health, due to the definite treatment of their oncologic problem (cure!). 8) Quality of life is good, due to the limited surgical trauma and adequate elimination of the reflux. 9) Morbidity and mortality are low. 10) Survival: after the procedure equals the general tumor-free population. Conclusions. Current concepts for limitation of the surgical approach seem justified, and superior to endoscopic approaches. Breast conserving therapy and oncoplastic procedures for centrally located breast cancer: oncologic and cosmetic outcome Methods. A recent definition proposed the following terminology: Encapsulated follicular carcinoma (with capsular invasion alone, with limited vascular invasion ( < 4), with extensive vascular invasion ( > 3) and widely invasive follicular carcinoma. In order to study the incidence and the prognosis of these various diagnostic groups, we analyzed all follicular carcinomas diagnosed within a 10-year period at the Kaiserin Elisabeth Spital, Vienna, Austria, the follow up time was at least 8 years. Results. In our study, we analyzed and reevaluated 44 patients with MIFTC: None of the patients experienced metastases, recurrent disease or tumor associated death. A detailed clinical and pathological work-up will be presented. Conclusions. The results of our study demonstrated an innocuous behavior of these tumor types which should be managed accordingly. Therefore, we conclude, that a limited therapeutic approach (i.e. no completion thyreoidectomy and no radioiodine treatment) is justified in minimally invasive follicular thyroid carcinoma. Background. Gastrointestinal stromal tumors (GIST) are the main mesenchymal neoplasmas in the gastrointestinal tract (GI), but represent less than 1% of all malignant GI-tumours. Tumour size and mitotic rate correlate with potential malignancy and frequency of recurrence. Additionally it seems that gastric GISTs have a more favourable outcome compared to tumors located in the intestine. Methods. Between 1998 and 2007 95 patients (43 female, median age 60.9 AE 14,2a) underwent surgical treatment for GIST. This study focuses mainly on extragastric GISTs (43 patients, 45.3%). Follow up investigations consisted of multislice CT. Results. The mean tumour size was 12.8 AE 9.3 cm, mainly located in the small bowel (44.2%), Colon=Rectum (25.6%) followed by the duodenum (16.3%). According to the Fletcher criteria 3 (7.0%) tumors were classified as very low risk, 10 (23.3%) low risk, 13 (30.2%) intermediate risk and 17 (39.5%) as high risk tumors. In 5 patients (11.6%) the immunhistologically staining was negative for c-kit. R0-Resection was achieved in 34 patients (79.1%), R1 in 5 (11.6%) and R2-Resection in 4 patients (9.3%). The median follow up period was 34.9 AE 24.5 months (median: 28.7 months). Fifteen operations in 10 patients (23.3%) were performed due to metastasis or recurrence. The recurrence rate in the gastric GIST population was 7% after R0 resection. Four patients (9.3%) were received Glivec due to recurrence of disease. Conclusions: Histologically proven complete resection is an effective treatment for GIST. Follow up investigations with multislice CT are recommended due to its potential malignant behaviour. Extragastric GISTs tend to show a higher potential for malignant behaviour. Ergebnisse. Die Gesamtmortalität von n ¼ 51 operierten Patienten betrug 4% (n ¼ 2). The long term outcome after stapled hemorrhoidopexy (Longo procedure) -Analysis of pain, recurrences and complications Background. Stapled Hemorrhoidopexy (SH) first described by Longo presents one of the most common operations for the treatment of hemorrhoids. However, more than a decade after its introduction data on the longterm outcome of SH is still scarce. This study was conducted to provide clincial findings on SH after an observation period of almost 10 years after surgery. Methods. Two hundred and nine patients who underwent SH between 1998 and 2001 at our department were invited for a clinical examination and to complete a questionnaire on patient satisfaction, pain and need for a re-operation. Patients who were unable to attend were asked to send back the completed questionnaire alone. The clinical inspection included a rectoscopy. Until December 2007 99 patients (48%) provided the questionnaire and 33 patients (14%) were clinically examined. For these 16 women and 17 men (mean age both: 61 years) the Wexner score was calculated. 49 patients (17%) could not be contacted (moved, deceased). Results. Of the 99 patients replying per mail 11 patients necessitated a re-operation for mariscas, while 1 patient underwent a second SH due to recurrence and 1 patient suffered from a recurrence but refused a surgical re-do. 28 out of the 33 clinically examined patients developed mariscas without clinical symptoms. Conclusions. SH is an effective and safe procedure with a low incidence of recurrences or complications after a long term observation period. Fusobacterium (F.) is a genus of obligately anaerobic, non spore forming gram-negative, filamentous bacteria, responsible for Lemierre's syndrome, periodontal disease and skin ulcers. The role of F. in coloproctology has not been described into detail, yet. Methods. The present study included all patients between 1. 1.2002 and 1.7.2007 managed in our institution, who had at least one culture positive for Fusobacterium spp. Clinical findings, sites of infection, comorbidities and outcome of the patients were assessed. Results. From 1. 1.2002 to 1.7.2007 a total of 211 cultures from 168 patients were found to be positive for Fusobacterium spp. In 70 patients fusobacterium was not further classified, F. varium was found in 54 (32.1%), F. nucleatum in 31 (18.5%), F. necrophorum in 12 (7.1%) and F. mortiferum in 1 (0.6%) patient, respectively. Conclusions. Fusobacterium spp. was present in a significant proportion of cultures taken from pilonidal sinus. The role of this anaerobic bacteria in pathogenesis of pilonidal sinus needs to be assessed in further studies.  A case of long-time untreated Crohn's disease resulting in a stenosis of the esophagus is described. The importance of an adequate therapy for Crohn's disease as well as the possible involvement of the esophagus is emphasized. A 46-years-old, male patient was presented to our surgery department with dysphagia, consisting for weeks. The patient was severely undernourished (BMI: 13.1) and in poor general condition. The patient's medical history showed Crohn's disease, which was diagnosed 15 years ago. After a period of adequate treatment, the patient decided to stop any further medication, because of a temporary renal insufficiency. Being asymptomatic for 10 years the patient then presented to our surgery department as described above. Diagnostic-wise we first implemented a gastroscopy, which showed a stenosis of the distal esophagus, impassable for the gastroscope. A parallel conducted CT scan displayed a circular wallthickening of major parts of the colon including the distal ileum, corresponding to a florid Crohn's disease. The histological result showed granulomas found beneath the epithelial layer, which indicated Crohn's disease in the gastroesophageal junction. Another gastroscopy with dilatation of the stenosis was performed, with good results in the upper GI X-ray and an improved general condition, the patient could be transferred to the department of internal medicine in order to restart his medication for Crohn's disease. Esophageal damage is an uncommon manifestation of Crohn's disease, but it should be considered in patients who have other intestinal manifestations of Crohn's disease and present with esophageal symptoms. Review on the novel Paull-Chandrasoma histopathology based definition of GERD and its clinical relevance. Results. Cardiac (CM), oxyntocardiac (OCM) and CM with intestinal metaplasia (IM ¼ Barrett's esophagus; BE) within biopsies obtained from the squamocolumnar junction (irrespective of endoscopic appearance and presence or absence of symptoms) results from reflux. Via a sequence including CM, IM, low-and high-grade dysplasia, adenocarcinoma of the esophagus may develop (annual incidence 0.5% for IM). Critical analysis of published data (Gastroenterology 2005; 129: 1825), using novel histopathology indicates that 10-16% of the normal population have BE. During the last 15 years frequency of esophageal adenocarcinoma increased 3.5 fold in Austria. Based on the novel concept, presence of GERD-symptoms and=or cancer risk (¼IM) defines disease, whereas absence of symptoms and=or cancer risk (OCM, CM) defines abnormality. Disease needs treatment (medical, endoscopic, surgical) and follow-up to exclude cancer risk (IM, low grade-, high grade dysplasia). Follow up for CM, IM and dysplasia is recommended in 5.3 and 0.25 years, respectively. A recent metaanalysis (Ann Surg 2007; 246: 11) indicates that effective fundoplication for Barrett's esophagus prevents cancer development. Management of dysplasia includes endoscopic mucosal resection, ablation and surgical resection. Abnormality is followed at 5-year intervals for exclusion of cancer risk development. Conclusions. Histopathology-based definition of GERD defines those at risk for esophageal cancer. Increasing evidence indicates that antireflux surgery prevents progression of Barrett's towards esophageal adenocarcinoma. Background. Malignant esophago-tracheal fistula represents a devastating complication of progressive esophageal carcinoma. The correct management still remains controversial but the priority objective should be to restore patient's respiratory and digestive function. We describe the case of a 60-year-old male patient suffering from esophageal carcinoma who had underwent photodynamic therapy, brachytherapy and esophageal stenting. Despite the induced multimodal therapy, a malignant fistula into the trachea developed 6 months later which could be sealed successfully by insertion of a covered metal bifurcation stent into the trachea. Methods. At re-admission the patient reported about coughing after swallowing, moderate dyspnea and slight fever for the last 14 days. Esophagogram, endoscopy and CT scan of the thorax revealed the fistula proximal to the tracheal bifurcation. Broad spectrum intravenous antibiotic treatment was initiated and oral intake was stopped. Implantation of a self-expandable covered metal bifurcation stent by flexible bronchoscopy could be performed without complications. Furthermore, a second esophageal stent was inserted in order to close the fistula from both sides. Physiotherapy, inhalation and mucolytic medication were administered in order to prevent clogging of the bifurcation stent. Results. Coughing, dyspnea and fever subsided after successfull stent implantation and oral intake of food was resumed on the next day when effectiveness of fistula occlusion had been documented by fluoroscopy. Conclusions. Palliative endoscopic insertion of a self-expandable covered metal bifurcation stent into the trachea represents a safe and effective approach resulting in immediate closure of the malignant esophago-tracheal fistula and leading to significant improvement of the patient's general condition. Meyer 2 ductal puncture, cholangiography was successful in 15=16 attempts (93.8%) versus pancreaticography in each case of 19 attempts (100%). While cholangiodrainage was achieved in 12=15 subjects (technical success rate, 80%), drain into the pancreatic duct was correctly placed in 11=15 individuals (73.3%) using the translumenal route. Though slight postinterventional pain was observed in each of the 30 cases, only cholangitis (n ¼ 1) and hemobilia (n ¼ 1) occurred after cholangiodrainage whereas after translumenal drainage of the pancreatic duct, perforation, pancreatitis (n ¼ 1 each) and bleeeding (n ¼ 2) were documented as severe postinterventional complications (periinterventional morbidity, 12.5% and 21.1%, resp.). Endoscopic reintervention rate was 25% and 18.2%, resp. (main cause, stent dislocation; intervention-related mortality, 0). Conclusions. Interventional endoscopic measures in pancreatic pseudocysts, abscesses and infected necroses U. Will 1 , C. Wanzar 1 , R. Gerlach 1 , F. Meyer 2 1 Municipal Hospital, Gera, Germany, 2 University Hospital, Magdeburg, Germany Background. To investigate feasibility=outcome of endoscopy-, ultrasound-and EUS-guided drainage of pancreatic pseudocysts and abscesses plus endoscopic debridement of infected necroses. Methods. All consecutive patients with symptomatic noninfected pseudocysts, abscesses and infected pancreatic necroses (inclusion criteria) were documented in this prospective single centre observational study (design, case series) using a computer-based data registry and approached with endoscopic interventions as the primary step. Feasibility was characterized with success and complication rate whereas outcome was assessed with periinterventional morbidity, mortality and recurrence rate revealed by intermediate follow-up investigation. Results. From 03=23=2002-09=23=2006, 87patients (sex ratio, females:males ¼ 24:63 [1:2.6]) with symptomatic non-infected pancreatic pseudocysts (n ¼ 22), abscesses (n ¼ 45) and infected necroses (n ¼ 20) were enrolled. Technical success rate in EUSguided transmural and ultrasound-guided external drainage was 100% (transpapillary drainage, 91.3%). While the interventionrelated complication rate in external drainage was 5.9%, this rate in transpapillary and transmural drainage was 0 and 8.1%, respectively. Late complications ( > 24 h) were observed in 6.5% of patients after transpapillary drainage (external drainage, 2.9%; transgastric drainage, 18.9%). Complications in 4 cases (bleeding, n ¼ 2; perforation, n ¼ 1; dislocation of the prosthesis with ileum perforation, n ¼ 1) needed to be approached surgically. After a mean follow-up period of 8.9 (range, 3-41) months, 12.2 (range, 3-56) months and 9.2 (range, 3-46) months, definitive therapeutic success rate was 95.4% in average for pseudocyst (95%), abscess (95%) and necrosis (95.5%), respectively (recurrence rate, 3.5%; mortality, 1.1%). All recurrent problems could be managed endoscopically. Conclusions. In the majority of cases, the consequent endoscopy-based management of pseudocysts, abscesses and infected necroses using transpapillary, ultrasound-guided external and EUS-guided transmural drainage plus endoscopic debridement is suitable and favorable also in daily clinical routine since it is a safe and efficacious approach in experienced hands. It primarily avoids the more traumatic surgical intervention, which remains as a final option if necessary. Ergebnisse. Wykypiel, R. Margreiter Background. Abdominal chylous cyst formation is a rare event, predominantly occurring after retroperitoneal surgery. The presented case is the first report in the literature of a chylous cyst formation following laparoscopic fundoplication. Methods. Report of a case. A 57-year-old man with a history of a spine compression fracture (T11=12) underwent laparoscopic fundoplication in 1996. After years he developed intermittent abdominal pain under the right costal margin. In 2002, a compression of the distal esophagus was found and a CT scan revealed a small cystic formation next to the distal esophagus. Further gastroscopies were normal and the patient therefore not followed. Pain continued with nausea, inappetence and weight loss. In 2006, he had escalating symptoms with weight loss. CT scan revealed a 7 cm cyst along the fundoplicate and the lesser curvature of the stomach. The cyst was drained laparoscopically. The drained fluid contained 35 mg=dl Cholesterol, 263 mg=dl LDL-Cholesterol, 334 mg=dl Triglycerides and Chylomicrones. The diagnosis chylous cyst was made and the patient was put on diet. After 12 weeks, the drain was removed after the discharge had stopped. The patient remained symptom-free for 7 months but then presented again with the same symptoms. This time a huge cyst was diagnosed, ranging from the lesser curvature of the stomach up to the right atrium. Surgical drainage was performed creating a Roux-en-Y chylouscysto-jejunostomy. The patient recovered uneventfully and is free of symptoms. Conclusions. A chylous cyst may develop after laparoscopic fundoplication which can be cured by drainage into a Roux-en-Y loop. Conclusions. Ligation of the appendix which is the cheaper option proved to be as safe as stapling without prolonging the operation time. One drawback of our study is the retrospective design. It remains unclear if in certain situations the stapling technique might be superior to ligation. The diagnosis and treatment of the Meckel diverticulum continue to fascinate abdominal surgeons. While the treatment of symptomatic diverticula follows established rules, appropriate and generally accepted criteria for incidentally found Meckel diverticula have not been formulated so far. Furthermore, the ''disease of the twos'' must be reconsidered in the context of emerging laparoscopic techniques. Methods. A meta-analysis of recent large studies reporting Meckel diverticula especially in adults was undertaken. Results. The morbidity and mortality of 1116 incidental resections were 3,67 and 0,18%, respectively, while after surgery for 502 symptomatic diverticula; a morbidity of 9.56% and a mortality of 1.99% were found. The difference is highly significant. All the series consistently report symptomatic cases at an advanced age. The usage of laparoscopy in diagnosis and treatment of the Meckel diverticulum, both symptomatic and asymptomatic, varies. Discussion. Incidental diverticulectomy can nowadays be performed with morbidity and mortality rates far below the rates for symptomatic cases. Therefore, we recommend active search for and removal of incidentally found Meckel diverticula, when surgically possible and reasonable, at any age. This recommendation is corroborated by an algorithm generated from the data of the most recent series. Conclusions. Diverticulectomy of an incidentally found Meckel diverticulum is (and will always be) up to the judgement of the individual surgeon, but a growing body of evidence can support this decision. The final value of laparoscopic techniques is still to be determined. One decade of an acute pain service (APS) in a large community hospital in Viennaa benchmarking project to optimize perioperative patient care Background. More than a decade ago PCA and regional anaesthetic procedures have been implemented in postop patients at our hospital and are surveilled by an acute pain service (APS). As only 10% of surgical patients are subjected to these techniques, the APS covers the perioperative pain management of the other 90% as well. Despite continous efforts to standardize and communicate the regimen of perioperative pain therapies and its managment at the wards limitations, the need for better translation to the clinical routine was observed even after 10 years. Methods. Based on voluntary participation of all surgical wards at our hospital a benchmarking project on the quality of postop pain care was initated in 2006. 524 ( ¼ n) patients were routinely assessed concerning satisfatcion and peri-and postoperative pain using the visual analogue scale (VAS). Results. Patient satisfatcion was good (range 1 to 1.91; mean value (MV): 1.39). The MV of all patients assessed with the VAS was 82% (at 3 wards 100%). A significant correlation between patient satisfatcion and intensity of pain with the repeated use of the VAS was observed. A significant reduction of pain (only 65% of patients reported < 3 [out of 10] on the VAS in 2004) was found in 2007 with 85% of patients reporting < 3 on the VAS. Conclusions. Peri-and postoperative pain management is a multidisciplinary task. The motivation of the staff involved seems to play a significant role in its quality and can be longlastingly improved by new stimulus, e.g. a competition between departments. Glaser 1 1 Department of Surgery II, Wilheminenspital, Wien, Austria; 2 Zentralröntgeninstitut, Wilheminenspital, Vienna, Austria Background. Intraabdominal gossypiboma (''gossipium'' ¼ cotton=''boma'' ¼ concealment) or intraabdominal textiloma are the result of a secondary reaction to textile material left in the abdominal cavity. Gossypiboma shows a morbidity of 50% and a mortality of 10%, but sometimes few or no complications occur. We present a 49-year-old man admitted to our department with an intraabdominal cystic tumor. Patient history. Twenty-four years ago the patient underwent a laparotomy with intestinal repair, following a gunshot wound in South America. Since then, there was no sign of bowel or urinary tract obstruction. Recently the patient reported a painless increase of abdominal diameter. Serologic testing for echinococcus and other parasites was negative. Ultrasound showed a cystic tumor with an undefined content. We suspected a large foreign body and performed an abdominal CT. The result was highly suspicious of Gossypiboma, without signs of infiltration of any intraabdominal organ. Operation. Relaparotomy with extirpation of the tumor, photo-documentation and pathological confirmation of Gossypiboma. Conclusions. In rare cases Gossypibomas do not cause problems and can mimic large intraabdominal tumors. Telemedicine is most frequently used to describe care-related applications while Telehealth or better e-Health encompasses other functions such as education and training, health promotion, public health, health services management, technical information retrieval, etc. Cybermedicine refers to the intersection of health and bioengineering, implantable intelligent hardware, automation of processes, robotics, biosensor nanotechnology, etc. In this presentation Telemedicine is used in its broadest possible scope including functions and applications of both e-health and Cybermedicine. eHealth, as defined by the European Commission -Information Society, ''includes systems and services improving access and quality and cost-efficiency of healthcare. The primary objectives focus on health and public health information networks, the use of electronic healthcare and insurance cards, extending the advances in telemedicine to the healthcare sector and the expansion of health and related preventative services to a Trans-European level.'' Intraoperatives Stentgraft zur Therapie einer Truncus coeliacus -Stenose bei pyloruserhaltender Duodenopancreatektomie J. Huber, F. Tomaselli, M. Gschwendtner, R. Függer Grundlagen. Die pyloruserhaltende Duodenopancreatektomie gilt als Standard in der Behandlung von malignen Pancreaskopftumoren. Koinzidente Stenosen am Truncus coeliacus sind selten und werden üblicherweise im Rahmen des präoperativen Stagings nicht erfasst. Sie stellen aber ein massives Risiko für eine Minderperfusion von Leber und Magen, sowie die konsekutive Entwicklung schwerer Komplikationen dar. Fallbericht. Wir präsentieren eine 67 jährige Patientin mit klinisch hochgradig malignomsuspektem Pancreaskopftumor. Das präoperative Staging ergab keinen Hinweis auf Inoperabilität. Die Resektion inklusive Standardlymphadenektomie erfolgte ohne Besonderheiten. Der intraoperative Gefrierschnitt bestätigte die Diagnose Pancreascarcinom. Während der Schnellschnittphase fielen eine livide Verfärbung der Leber, des Magens, sowie ein deutlich abgeschwächter Puls im Truncus coeliacus auf. Die intraoperative Duplexsonographie ergab den Verdacht auf eine höchstgradige, kurzstreckige Truncus coeliacus -Stenose, welche zunächst angiographisch bestätigt und anschließend interventionell angiographisch dilatiert und gestentet wurde. Es konnte sofort eine adäquate Reperfusion erzielt werden. Die Operation wurde mit der Rekonstruktionsphase in typischer Art und Weise fortgesetzt und komplikationsfrei beendet. Postoperativ imponierte ein deutliches Reperfusionssyndrom mit erhöhter GOT ( > 15000 U=l), GPT ( > 6000 U=l) und LDH ( > 8000 U=l), sowie eine 2 Wochen anhaltende Magenatonie. Eine komplette Restitutio ad integrum konnte nach 3 Wochen verzeichnet werden. Histologisch ergab sich ein mäßig differenziertes ductales Carcinom des Caput pancreatis, pT3 pN1 (9=20) R0 mit einer koinzidenten perifokalen Pancreatitis. Schlussfolgerungen. Perfusionstörungen durch eine Truncus coeliacus-Stenose sind seltene, aber potentiell risikoreiche Komplikationen bei Duodenopancreatektomien. Bei intraoperativer Diagnose kann das Problem interventionell angiographisch beseitigt und damit die Entwicklung eines Leberversagens oder einer Anastomoseninsuffizienz als Folge der Minderperfusion verhindert werden. Grundlagen. Die akute mesenteriale Ischämie (AMI) weist trotz vielerlei Fortschritte in Diagnostik und Therapie in den letzten Jahrzehnten nach wie vor eine sehr hohe Letalität von 60 bis über 90% auf. Dieser Umstand ist vor allem auf die verspätete Diagnosestellung (die vor allem durch das sehr unspezifische klinische Erscheinungsbild der AMI bedingt ist) zurückzuführen. Methodik. Seit März 2003 werden alle Patienten erfasst, die in unserer chirurgischen Klinik aufgrund einer mesenterialen Ischämie operiert werden. Ergebnisse. Die hierbei erhobenen Daten beinhalten die unterschiedlichen Ä tiologien, Symptome und Laborparameter bei der initialen Untersuchung, die weiterführende bildgebende Diagnostik sowie die jeweilige Art und Anzahl der durchgeführten Operationen. Unterschieden werden gefäßchirurgische Interventionen (Embolektomien, Bypässe) und Darmresektionen sowie geplante und nicht geplante Revisionsoperationen. Die Lokalisation des Gefäßverschlusses (einschließlich des betroffenen Darmabschnittes) eines jeden Patienten wird ebenso erfasst wie begleitende, nicht-viszerale thrombembolische Geschehnisse. Ein weiterer Gesichtspunkt befasst sich mit der Art der Aufnahme in unsere Klinik, um die Bedeutung des Faktors Zeit hervorzuheben: hatten hier Patienten, die aus anderen Kliniken verlegt wurden eine eine signifikant schlechtere Prognose als Patienten, die sich mit akuten abdominellen Schmerzen direkt in der Ambulanz vorstellten. Schlussfolgerungen. Um die Letalität der mesenterialen Ischämie zu senken, ist eine enge interdisziplinäre, klinikübergreifende Zusammenarbeit nötig, um die Diagnostik zügig in die richtigen Bahnen zu lenken und so die Einleitung der operativen Therapie zu beschleunigen. Hier sind neben den behandelnden Fachrichtungen wie Anästhesisten, Viszeral-und Gefäßchirurgen und Internisten auch sämtliche anderen Disziplinen betroffen, die an der Akutversorgung von Patienten mitwirken. Durch den Einsatz des Lasers kam es zu keinen nachteiligen Ereignissen. Endovenöse Laserablation als minimal invasive Alternative zum Stripping der Vena saphena magna M. Kalteis 1;2 , I. Berger 2 , S. Messie-Werndl 2 , R. Pistrich 2 , W. Schimetta 3 , W. Pölz 3 , F. Hietler 2 Grundlagen. In den letzten Jahren wurden verschiedene minimal invasive Alternativen zum Stripping der insuffizienten Vena saphena magna entwickelt. Von diesen hat die endovenöse Laserablation (EVL) die größte Verbreitung erfahren und wird von manchen Anwendern bereits als Methode der Wahl angeboten. Wir stellen unsere Ergebnisse einer randomisierten, kontrollierten Studie zum Vergleich von EVL und Stripping -jeweils mit Crossektomie -vor. Methodik. Einhundert Patienten mit typischer Stammvarikose der Vena saphena magna, die für beide Behandlungsmethoden geeignet waren, wurden in die Therapiegruppen Stripping oder EVL randomisiert. Nachuntersuchungen erfolgten nach 1, 4 und 16 Wochen. Als primäre Endpunkte wurden die Hämatomfläche und der Verlauf des krankheitsspezifischen CIVIQ Lebensqualitätsscores untersucht. Sekundäre Endpunkte waren die Verschlussrate der Vena saphena magna, Komplikationen, Schmerz und Analgetikaverbrauch, Zufriedenheit mit dem kosmetischen Ergebnis und Krankenstandsdauer. Ergebnisse. Die Hämatomfläche nach EVL erwies sich als signifikant kleiner (125 cm 2 vs. 200 cm 2 , p ¼ 0,001), der Verlauf des Lebensqualitätsscores zeigte keinen signifikanten Unterschied. Die sekundären Endpunkte ergaben sehr gute Ergebnisse in beiden Gruppen mit einer 100% Erfolgsrate (Verschluss=Entfernung der Vene). Die Unterschiede zwischen den Gruppen waren insgesamt nur gering und ohne klinische Relevanz bzw. großteils ohne statistische Signifikanz. Aus der Literatur ergeben sich Hinweise, dass die EVL bei einer deutlichen Minimierung des Eingriffes (Weglassen der Crossektomie, Ablation nur am Oberschenkel, Reduktion der Miniphlebektomien) bessere Ergebnisse bezüglich des Patientenkomforts ergibt. Schlussfolgerungen. Die Lebensqualität nach EVL ist gleichwertig, die postoperative Hämatombildung ist geringer im Vergleich zum Stripping. Die Langzeitergebnisse der EVL mit und ohne Crossektomie sollten in weiteren Studien untersucht werden. Mutliple viszerale Embolien auf dem Boden einer tiefen Beinvenethrombose - Grundlagen. Die mesenteriale Ischämie ist eine Erkrankung aus dem Symptomenkreis des akuten Abdomens mit einem mannigfaltigen klinischen Erscheinungsbild. Am vorliegenden Fall soll die Notwenigkeit unverzüglicher Diagnostik und Therapie, auch bereits bei bloßen Verdacht auf ein thrombembolisches Geschehen der Viszeralgefäße, auch bei fehlenden Risikofaktoren (hohes Alter, Arryhthmia absoluta, . . .) demonstriert werden. Fallbericht. Ein 49 jähriger, männlicher Patient ohne bekannte Vorerkrankungen wurde in einer auswärtigen Klinik zwei Wochen zuvor bei tiefer Beinvenenthrombose links und Lungenembolie beidseits aufgenommen und therapeutisch heparinisiert. Nachdem es zu einer Verschlechterung des Allgemeinzustandes kam, erfolgte die Verlegung in die Medizinische Klinik im Hause. Kurz nach Eintreffen in der Medizinischen Klinik bot der Patient das Bild eines akuten Abdomens, woraufhin eine sofortige Vorstellung in unserer chirurgischen Klinik erfolgte. In der initital durchgeführten Computertomographie des Abdomens zeigte sich neben einer Embolie des Truncus coeliacus und der A. mesenterica superior auch eine Embolie der A. renalis sinistra mit Ischämiezeichen der Milz und der linken Niere. Der Patient wurde sofort laparotomiert und es wurde eine Embolektomie der A. mesenterica superior und der A. renalis sinistra durchgeführt. Durch eine intraoperativ veranlasste TEE konnte der Verdacht auf eine paradoxe Embolie bestätigt werden. In gleicher Sitzung wurde daher zum Schutz vor erneuten postoperativen Embolien ein Cava-Schirmchen durch die Radiologen eingesetzt. Nach kurzem intensivmedizinischen Aufenthalt konnte der Patient auf Normalstation verlegt werden. Sämtliche von der Ischämie betroffenen Viszeralorgane erholten sich ohne weitere Folgen laborchemisch von der Ischämiezeit und zeigten in den folgenden sonographischen Kontrollen Normalbefunde. Weitere emblolische Ereignisse traten nicht auf. Results. Over 2 years, 5 patients (m=f ¼ 4:1; mean age, 63 years) underwent an operation at visceral arteries out of 1118 vasculosurgical interventions in total. Duplexsonography, angiography and multislice CT scan revealed a combined occlusion of the coeliac trunk and the superior mesenteric artery (SMA) in 4 cases (additionally, stenosis of the inferior mesenteric artery (IFA), n ¼ 1). In the 5th case, there was an isolated occlusion at the SMA-origin. The aortomesenteric reconstruction was subdivided according to: i) target vessel (combination of common hepatic artery and SMA with an autologous Y-vein bypass, n ¼ 2; venous patch at the IFA-origin, n ¼ 1; prosthetic bypass to the SMA from the iliacal segment of a previously implanted bifurcational prosthesis, n ¼ 2); ii) bypass origin (from the supracoeliac aortic segment, n ¼ 3 [antegrade] versus the infrarenal segment, n ¼ 2 [retrograde]). Significant improval of the quality of life was observed (increase of body weight, no further abdominal angina; n ¼ 5 each) and primary wound healing (n ¼ 4; VAC-therapy in prolongated wound healing after surgical reintervention, n ¼ 1). In this case, an ischemic jejunal segment needed to be resected (10 cm). In the case with autologous venous patch at the IFAorigin, postoperative occlusion of the supracoeliac venous bypass to the SMA was found (no signs=symptoms), but with sufficient perfusion via the reconstructed IFA (hospital mortality, 0%). Conclusions. Antegrade supracoeliac aortomesenteric revascularization is favourable in mesenteric ischemia because of the sustained physiological direction of blood flow þ the more feasible approach to the target vessel. Vasculäre Leiomyosarkome: Diagnostik, Therapie und Prognose Vasculäre Leiomyosarkome (LMS) sind seltene Weichteiltumore, welche von der Gefäßwandmedia ihren Ausgang nehmen. Wegen uncharakteristischer Symptome erfolgt die Diagnosestellung meist erst im fortgeschrittenen Stadium, so dass eine primär kurative Operation oft nicht mehr möglich ist. Am häufigsten finden sich vasculäre LMS in den großen Venen vor allem der V. Cava, wesentlich seltener in der Pulmonalarterie oder in großen Arterien. Wir berichten über 3 Patienten mit vasculären LMS der Vena Cava inferior. Symptomatik, Diagnostik, Therapie und Prognose werden anhand von Fallberichten und der aktuellen Literatur diskutiert. Background. When about 10 years ago, gastric banding was introduced as a bariatric operation its early results were promising with a low complication rate. Only few long-term studies have been published. In this study we assessed our results of laparoscopic gastric banding in young patients after up to 10 years. Methods. Between January 1996 and December 2000, a total of 41 patients (83% female, 17% male) aged younger than 25 years underwent laparoscopic gastric banding at our institution. Patients' data were derived from the electronic patient data system, paper charts and by means of a telephone questionnaire. The psychosocial changes were analyzed by using Moorehead-Ardelt=BAROS questionnaire. Results. Mean preoperative BMI was 44.26 AE 6.53 kg=m 2 with a mean EW of 65.22 AE 20.48 kg. BMI after 1, 5 and 7 years was 31.50 AE 7.38 kg=m 2 , 31.12 AE 7.10 kg=m 2 and 32.88 AE 5.68 kg= m 2 . Mean EWL after 1 year was 60.07 AE 25.33%, after 5 and 7 years EWL was 64.84 AE 27.45% and 57.48 AE 28.07%. An improvement in obesity-related co-morbidities was observed in nearly all patients. Out of our patients 52% had complications requiring reoperation (27% pouch dilations, 10% band leakages, 5% intragastral band migrations, 5% perforation of the esophagus and 5% port disconnections). According to BAROS, the long-term outcome was regarded as ''failure'' in 40%, ''fair'' in 4%, ''good'' in 28%, ''very good'' in 20% and ''excellent'' in 8%. Conclusions. Our mid-term results show disappointing results with a high complication rate and many dissatisfied patients. While surgery and radiation therapy still present the treatment of choice for many advanced tumors, our increased insight into the molecular working of the transformation process makes molecularly-targeted therapies a feasible alternative. The seri-ne=threonine kinases C-and B-RAF are frequently affected in human tumors. Despite the development of small molecular weight RAF inhibitors (Sorafenib, Nexavar), benefits for patients have been very limited. The reasons for this may be multiple, including the complexity of mutational changes usually observed in tumors, whose individual or joint contribution to the establishment and maintenance of the tumor are still poorly understood. Mutations in the RAS-RAF-MEK-ERK pathway frequently coincide with deregulation of the PI-3-Kinase=Protein kinase B (PI3K=PKB) pathway. To gain further insights into a possible RAF=PKB cooperation in transformation we analyzed activated RAF and PI3K=PKB individually for their effects on various aspects of transformation and probed into a possible RAF effector function of PI3K=PKB. Using established fibroblast and human melanoma cell lines we demonstrate that (i) RAF and PKB cooperate in the transformation of fibroblasts; (ii) both signaling entities contribute to proliferation and survival of transformed cells, and (iii) inhibitors of PI3K=PKB severely affect growth and survival of RAF-transformed cells lacking mutations in PI3K=PKB. Taken together, these data suggest that PI3K=PKB may constitute valid therapeutic targets in tumors carrying RAF mutations. PSMA: Ein potentielles Target für eine angiogenetische Therapie beim kolorektalen Karzinom Grundlagen. Nach einer Ruptur des vorderen Kreuzbandes besteht neben einer mechanischen eine durch ein sensomotorisches Defizit bedingte funktionelle Instabilität. Zur Untersuchung der funktionellen Instabilitätskomponente kann man sich den Reflexbogen zwischen VKB und den Hamstrings von Nutzen machen. Ziel dieser Studie war es, zu untersuchen inwieweit sich eine Kreuzbandverletzung auf das Reflexverhalten insbesondere auf die SLR (Short Latency Response) und die MLR (Medium Latency Response) auswirkt. Methodik. Hierzu wurden bei 21 Patienten mit isolierter Kreuzbandruptur die SLR und MLR nach mechanisch provozierter ventraler Tibiatranslation via EMG aufgezeichnet und hinsichtlich der Latenzzeiten untersucht. Die Bestimmung der SLR und MLR erfolgt hierbei mithilfe eines Testverfahrens, dass eigens hierfür in Voruntersuchungen entwickelt wurde. Innerhalb des Patientenkollektives erfolgte die Einteilung der Patienten mit ,,Giving way'' Symptomatik (n ¼ 12, Non-Coper) und ohne ,,Giving way'' Symptomatik (n ¼ 9, Coper). Für die Latenz der MLR konnte eine signifikante Unterschied zwischen gesundem und verletztem Bein gefunden werden (p < 0.001). Ergebnisse. Es konnte gezeigt werden, dass eine VKB-Ruptur zu einer signifikanten Verlängerung der ischiocruralen Reflexaktivität und zu einer signifikanten Zunahme der anterioren Tibiatranslation führt. Der Vergleich zwischen den Non-Copern und Copern ergab auf der gesunden Seite keine signifikante Veränderung hinsichtlich der SLR=MLR Latenzzeiten. Auf der verletzten Seite konnte jedoch eine signifikant verlängerte MLR für die Non-Coper festgestellt werden (p < 0.05). Schlussfolgerungen. Es ist somit von einem direkten Zusammenhang zwischen einer ,,Giving way'' Symptomatik und einer gestörten sensomotorischen Ansteuerung auszugehen, die mit einer Veränderung der MLR einhergeht. Im Vergleich mit anderen Sepsis-Modellen, im Speziellen mit dem bisher realitätstreuesten Modell (CLP ¼ Colon ligation puncture), zeigt die CASP eindeutig Vorteile. Der große Vorteil des CASP-Modells beruht darauf, dass das intra-abdominelle Geschehen exakt dem einer Perforation oder Anastomosen-Dehiszenz gleicht. Ein weiteres wesentliches Argument besteht darin, dass der Zytokinverlauf der Sepsis im Mausmodell dem Zytokinverlauf des Menschen entspricht. Ein Nachteil dieses Modells besteht in der relativ langwierigen Lernkurve. Durch die Etablierung dieses realitätsnahen Sepsis-Modells in Forschungszentren kann in Zukunft im Bereich der Peritonitis und Sepsis eine optimale Grundlagenforschung betrieben werden. Einerseits kann molekular-biologisch die Pathophysiologie der Sepsis weiter erforscht werden, andererseits kann versucht werden mit neuen Therapieansätzen auf die Mortalität der Sepsis Einfluss zu nehmen. Insgesamt ein interessantes Peritonitismodell dessen Stärken und Schwächen wir im vergleich zu anderen Modellen aufzeigen wollen. The impact of different barriers in experimental IPOM hernia repair using a polypropylene mesh Background. Meshes as well as fixation devices in intraperitoneal onlay mesh plastic technique (IPOM) can evoke adhesions. Various implant designs are available and can be divided in coated and uncoated products. Most of these antiadhesive barriers (AB) are also available separately to cover uncoated products. The presented study design combining one type of mesh with different AB (providing a barrier between implant and viscera until the mesh is covered by neomesothelium) rules out a possible impact of different mesh materials. Methods. Thirty-two rats were operated in open IPOM technique (n ¼ 8 per group). One mesh per animal (2Â 2 cm) was fixed Schlussfolgerung. Österreichische Gesellschaft für Thorax-und Herzchirurgie P111 Unilateral pulmonary artery occlusion: differential diagnosis and treatment strategies M. Hoda, S. Taghavi, P. Jaksch, C. Aigner, G. Lang, I. Lang, W. Klepetko Background. Unilateral total pulmonary artery (PA) occlusion is a rare finding. Its etiology includes chronic thromboembolic (CTEPH), tumorous and systemic inflammatory diseases. The aim of this retrospective study was to analyse incidence and clinical course of this entity in an institutional cohort of patients referred for pulmonary endarterectomy (PEA). Methods. Nine patients (6 women and 3 men, mean age 36.4 AE 12.1 [range 20 to 56]) with unilateral total PA occlusion were identified among 162 patients referred for PEA between 1992 and 2006 (incidence 5.5%). All occlusions were on the right side. Etiology was CTEPH in 6 patients, angiosarcoma of the PA in 2 and Takayasu's arteritis in 1 patient. PEA was performed in 6 patients (including rePEA in one patient) and was accompanied by lobectomy in 1 patient. The remaining 3 patients underwent angiosarcoma resection in 2 and biopsy in 1 patient. Results. Seven patients are alive with a mean follow up of 49.8 AE 40.1 months (11 to 109, median 42). The 5 patients with primary PEA had an excellent hemodynamically improvement, the patient with rePEA had only partial reopening of the PA and died on the lung transplant waiting list. The 2 patients with angiosarcoma had complete reopening of the PA, underwent adjuvant chemoradiatiotherapy, one patient died 24 months after operation. The patient with takayasu's arteritis was treated with immunsuppressive therapy. Conclusions. Unilateral total PA occlusion is a rare finding which needs a thoroughful preoperative workup. Extracorporeal circulation in CABG procedures in patients < and >80 years -Is there a difference? N. Reiss, U. Schuett, A. Bairaktaris, R. Körfer Clinic for Thoracic and Cardiovascular Surgery, Heart Center North Rhine-Westphalia, Ruhr-University of Bochum, Bad Oeynhausen, Germany Background. In cardiac surgery pts. become older and older over the last decades. We have investigated in a retrospective study whether there are special differences and requirements in terms of extracorporeal circulation in pts. > 80 years. Methods. Statistical analysis was performed using SPSS for Windows 11.0. There were following significance levels: p < 0.05 significance, p < 0.01 high significance and p < 0.001 highest significance. In a ten year period 21.750 isolated CABG procedures were performed using heart-lung-machine. 20.986 pts. (96.5%, group A) were 80 years. 8.8% of procedures were urgent in group A, in group B 12.4% of operations were under urgent conditions. Results. In group A the number of performed bypass grafts was significantly higher than in group B. In consequence, bypass and cross-clamp-time was significantly shorter in group B. 75% of group A received no foreign blood units. In contrast, 75% of group B underwent foreign blood substitution to reach adequate hemoglobin levels. At least, in-hospital mortality did not differ in both groups. Conclusions. From our experience we conclude that performing CABG characteristics of patients < and > 80 years sig-nificantly differ. Nevertheless, clinical outcome is similar in both groups. For optimal perfusion management following parameters are of importance: adequate haemoglobin, minimal priming volume, minimal system surface, physiological arterial pressure and minimal hemolysis. Minimized ECC may help to reach these conditions, esp. in pts. > 80 years. Minimally invasive closure of an intercostal hernia using VATS mesh technique Background. Intercostal hernia is a rare complication after lateral thoracotomy for lung resection and occurs in less then 1% of cases. In reports on minimally invasive coronary artery bypass surgery the complication is described more often. The typical method of repair is a secondary closure of the intercostals space with firm non-absorbable sutures. Methods. We describe the case of a patient with a hernia in the fifth intercostal space after resection of a harmatoma through an anterolateral minithoractomy. The closure of the defect could be managed by video assisted thoracic surgery (VATS) using a nonabsorbable mesh placed over the defect and stapled to the adjacent ribs. Results. The postoperative course was uneventful. One year after the procedure the patient is free of recurrence and pain. Conclusions. Closure of a defect caused by an intercostal hernia can be managed by means of minimally invasive technique using a non-absorbable mesh.
